Continued Arrest of Robbers from the Sheng An Steamer 20

Seamen Escaping the Danger Recount the Tragic Incident

(Dalian) Two more escaped criminals from the Sheng An tragedy were arrested at 8:00 PM tonight. One is Gao Ziqi, a Swiss national, and the other is Miller, a German national. (2nd Reuters dispatch)

(Dalian) The remaining two escaped criminals from the Sheng An tragedy are still being actively pursued. The 58 Chinese seamen and coolies on the ship, after a night of peaceful sleep, have calmed their frightened spirits. One of them told a Reuters reporter today that the Sheng An ran aground on a reef 100 yards from Xingpu due to the thieves' careless navigation. At that time, he knew salvation had arrived, and he was extremely happy. He then recounted the entire story of the thieves' atrocities, saying that on June 25th, five foreigners requested the captain at Tangzhan to allow them to travel to Shanghai. Around 10:00 PM on the 28th, about 200 miles from Shanghai, the five men were stationed at key points on the ship. One of them suddenly opened fire, killing the Chinese radio operator and destroying the radio equipment. The first mate, Hosi Nanov, heard the gunfire and rushed to the deck, but bullets rained down on him, and he died instantly. Mr. Hosina's wife was chatting with Captain Wickman in the cabin when the thieves fired wildly through the window, killing both of them. Before the incident, Mrs. Ho had summoned the captain's Chinese servant. When the Chinese servant and another Chinese servant arrived, they were also killed by the thieves. Three Russians and three Chinese all died violently within seconds. The thieves then killed three Chinese seamen on the deck and two others who were sleeping soundly. Because the shots were so close, the heads of these two were almost blown off. The thieves then tied up the bodies with ropes and threw them into the sea. The three thieves who have been arrested now give the same account as above, and they also said that Captain Wickman was a burly man, making it very difficult to throw his body into the sea. Most of the other seamen were gambling at mahjong in the lower deck. Hearing the alarm, they turned pale and hid in a small room, tightly closing the door. There was no food or water in the room, and breathing was difficult, but everyone preferred to suffocate in the room rather than go outside. It was not until the ship ran aground that they saw the light of day again. Those seamen who did not have time to escape all suffered cruel treatment. The thieves ordered the ship to turn back towards Dalian. The thieves must have been to the port before. The thieves then ordered the words "Sheng An" to be painted over with lacquer and renamed "Hua Li." The two words "Hua Li" are still clearly visible today. The Sheng An ran aground at 3:00 AM on July 1st. All the seamen on the ship were then imprisoned. Four thieves first went ashore in two sampans. Westerman (initially reported as Weston) and Signa were arrested in a house, where they were sleeping with guns under their pillows. The leader, Daoding, left the ship a little later and was arrested when he landed. This was because the police, seeing the Sheng An, suspected it was a ship smuggling sugar and had gathered on the beach to investigate. Although the three thieves all carried German passports when they were arrested, they all claimed to be American citizens. (2nd Reuters dispatch)

Those Advocating Anti-Japanese Sentiment Are Not Allowed to Enter the Country

(Tokyo) Professor Currans of the University of Washington in the United States is about to travel to Japan. Ma Yinchu Discusses the Pros and Cons of Cotton and Wheat Loans 23

(Nanjing) Ma Yinchu spoke to reporters on the 2nd about the pros and cons of cotton and wheat loans as follows: ㈠ American cotton has long fibers and is clean, making it popular with yarn factories. However, American cotton costs about 60 yuan per dan in Chinese currency, while Chinese cotton costs only 46 yuan, which is cheaper. Yarn factories demand to buy at an 80% discount and be exempt from import duties. According to the cotton loan of 40 million US dollars, 900,000 bales can be purchased, which is similar to the amount of cotton imported by customs last year. If foreign cotton is no longer imported in the future, it seems to have little adverse impact on Chinese merchants. ㈡ The government issues bonds at about a 60% discount, while cotton loans are sold at an 80% discount, which is still a good deal. However, tariff exemptions are absolutely not allowed because central tax revenue will decrease, and Chinese cotton will also lose its protection. ㈢ The last time American wheat was borrowed, due to inconvenient transportation in the provinces along the Yangtze River, the relief wheat was sold in Shanghai, which made Shanghai wheat cheaper and the price of wheat in disaster areas higher. This time, the disaster areas are far away in Shaanxi and Gansu, and the transportation of relief grain is even more difficult. It is feared that the same mistake will be repeated, which is worrying. ㈣ The repayment period is too short. If exports are not increased or imports are not reduced, the exchange rate will inevitably plummet due to the excessive need for foreign exchange, and the losses will be great. Therefore, the use of loans should be limited to productive enterprises to avoid this problem. ㈤ In recent years, the Shanghai silver industry has found it difficult to issue loans, and investing in yarn factories is the only way out. Now that this road is closed, idle funds may flow into speculation, and social economy will increase several times. Losses should be paid attention to. ㈥ Farmers should improve their knowledge and not be greedy for small profits and mix impurities and water into Chinese cotton, causing them to lose the welcome of yarn factories, so that they can resist foreign cotton. (2nd Central News Agency dispatch)

Ministry of Communications Plans to Establish an Electrical Machinery Manufacturing Plant 24

Capital of Four Million Yuan

(Nanjing) Because the materials required for telecommunications administration have always been largely dependent on imported goods, and the outflow of interests is alarming, the Ministry of Communications has the original Shanghai Telecommunications Manufacturing Plant, but the scale is too small, and the products are trivial. Now it plans to establish a large-scale electrical machinery manufacturing plant, named the Central Electrical Machinery Manufacturing Plant, with a capital of four million yuan. The fund-raising methods are: first, the ministry issues short-term bonds; second, various banking groups invest; and third, loans are borrowed from the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Fund. This plan is currently being drafted in the Department of Telecommunications Administration and will be submitted to the ministerial meeting soon. The future factory site will be decided in Shanghai. (2nd Special dispatch)

Current Commentary

Another Difficulty for the World Economic Conference Ming 63

The World Economic Conference has been in session for three weeks since it officially opened on June 12. The biggest obstacle currently facing it is the war debt problem. Not only can it not be resolved satisfactorily, but it is also afraid to be mentioned openly. Although the British Prime Minister clearly stated in his opening remarks that the world economy would be difficult to recover if war debts were not resolved, there was no proper solution after the United States expressed its refusal. In order to maintain its credibility and leave room for future maneuvering, Britain had to pay a portion of the war debts due, but this was enough to cause agitation among European countries. Moreover, nationalism is now prevalent. Although it has been fully proven theoretically and practically that international cooperation is necessary for the world economy to recover, and that the widespread economic panic has no end, all countries in the world are confused by their own immediate interests and are unwilling to sacrifice for mutual benefit. Since this main issue is of different interests, and from war debts down, the so-called currency problem, tariff problem, and market development problem are all "self-righteous" and lack sincerity in cooperation. This is why, after three weeks of the conference, it is still impossible to find a ray of hope for cooperation.

The general opinion is that this war debt problem should be temporarily set aside because it conflicts too much, and the secondary currency stability problem should be solved first. If a stable international currency method can be found, then international trade may reach a balanced state, and economic panic may be slightly reduced. The ruined market can also be revitalized by this. It is also not the beginning of no plan, but since the financial panic in the United States, it has stopped the gold standard and has to adopt a policy of currency inflation to stimulate prices. As a result of the implementation of this policy, first, the European gold standard countries feel the threat of a large influx of American goods and cash outflow. Second, the domestic market in the United States will be completely filled with its own manufactured goods, and goods from other countries cannot be imported. As a result, Europe and the United States are opposed to each other, and the conflict between France and the United States cannot be reconciled, and other countries cannot be relieved. The so-called currency stability is not only a competition between the gold standard and the non-gold standard. Even countries that have abandoned the gold standard cannot but be wary of the American inflation policy.

The European countries led by France, in terms of political relations, Germany has formed another group, but economically, it still cannot be separated from France. The Netherlands, Switzerland, and other countries are even less likely to be separated. From our observation, the reasons why France maintains the gold standard system are: first, to maintain its absolute leadership position in the European financial community. France's cash reserves exceed 3.2 billion US dollars. Although it is dead in the vault, it has been valued by European countries. Since the United States abandoned the gold standard, France's position in Europe will increase. Second, if the currency parity is reduced, it will be beneficial to Britain, and after excessive inflation, France, with its inferior industry, will find it difficult to restrict the large-scale import of foreign manufactured goods. Therefore, the so-called stability of currency is to prevent excessive inflation policy, and it is also to maintain France's advantage.

The reason why the United States has reversed the previous Republican Party's actions and adopted a policy of currency inflation, focusing solely on the interests of industrial capital, is that it has already learned that the freezing of war debts is inevitable. In this time of industrial decline and agricultural recession, it is difficult to maintain the prosperity of its domestic market by relying solely on gold profits. Therefore, the current coping policy is to reduce the value of currency and increase prices through currency inflation in order to restore the market. The meaning of this is about two points. One is to stimulate general consumption power and encourage its foreign exports. Second, American products have not been able to keep pace with Japan in overseas markets due to the high value of the US dollar, and are even lagging behind Britain. Therefore, it has to depreciate its currency to make American goods re-enter the stage of commodity competition in order to transform the decline of its economic panic.

As for Britain and Japan, they have long abandoned the gold standard, and their currencies now have relative stability. Therefore, in the competition for currency stability between France and the United States, they pretend to be neutral. In fact, no matter what the future trend is, they can all obtain some benefits. In short, the principle of "currency stability" will not be fully implemented even if the United States accepts it. Moreover, the prices of the international market are especially not resolved by the formal agreement on the conference table. Therefore, even if the current difficulty of the economic conference can be overcome, there are still many future disasters. The optimistic component is particularly scarce.

The fate of the World Economic Conference is decided today

Roosevelt Rejects Currency Stabilization Plan 64

Hull to Explain U.S. Policy Today

Further Revisions Sought to European Proposal

French Delegation Sees Hope for Compromise

(London) U.S. President Roosevelt has rejected the European proposal for central bank cooperation to stabilize currencies but has left room for further negotiations, claiming he opposes the existing form of the plan. With Roosevelt's statement and Secretary of State Hull's announcement that he will elaborate on U.S. monetary policy at the economic conference on Monday, the initial disappointment at the rejection has been somewhat mitigated.

Undersecretary of State Moley, in preparation for the U.S. delegation's statement, will meet with leaders of major European delegations. French Finance Minister Bonnet has returned to Paris but is expected back in London on Monday to hear the U.S. delegation's statement and participate in possible negotiations.

Secretary of State Hull has not yet indicated the nature of the U.S. delegation's statement. Many representatives of gold standard countries believe that the U.S. will declare its desire to achieve absolute monetary equality in foreign trade, as countries that have devalued their currencies have gained valuable trade advantages for the past two years. Therefore, the U.S. President does not want to participate in strict stabilization efforts until the U.S. obtains equal benefits. However, Hull is expected to endorse a plan to stop speculative surges and declines.

While the French delegation assures that gold standard countries will adhere to their original proposal, it also believes there is still hope for compromise. A French delegate stated that President Roosevelt's rejection is not surprising, but if the U.S. insists on major modifications, the new plan may be of little benefit, as the current plan is already as moderate as possible. The original proposal of the gold standard countries has been repeatedly modified at the request of the British, and he does not know how much more can be modified at this point.

The Original Proposal Has Been Published, Part of Which Is as Follows 65

"Joint Declaration of Gold Standard and Non-Gold Standard Countries: It is hereby agreed that the international currency market should be stabilized as soon as practicable and to the greatest extent possible, and that this is in the common interest of all countries concerned. It is also agreed that the re-establishment of gold as the basis for calculating international exchange rates should be completed within the time deemed necessary by countries that have abandoned the gold standard to stabilize their currencies. The exchange rates with other currencies must be determined by the respective governments. The gold standard countries reiterate their knowledge of the current gold parity and the monetary laws of their respective countries, maintain the free use of the gold standard, and believe that maintaining the current gold parity is beneficial to the world's recovery. The countries that have abandoned the gold standard and are participating in this declaration will pay attention to the aforementioned declaration and acknowledge its importance, but this declaration does not prevent their future currency parity with gold, and they will reiterate that the ultimate goal of their monetary policy is to restore an international standard based on gold under appropriate conditions. The governments that have abandoned the gold standard agree to adopt the most effective measures to restrict exchange speculation. Other signatory countries will cooperate for the same purpose. The signatory governments agree to have their central banks cooperate with the central banks of other countries that have signed this declaration to limit speculation and, at the appropriate time, to rebuild an international gold standard."

U.S. Advocates for Revisions 66

Hull to Explain to the Conference Today

It is now expected that Hull will explain on Monday which parts of this draft declaration are not satisfactory to the U.S. Yesterday, the U.S. President stated at his summer retreat that he saw no reason to oppose central banks stopping speculation, so it is expected that he will agree on this point.

As for the gold standard countries, although they will insist on their position, it is said that they will not issue a declaration until Bonnet returns to England, and they will likely study the U.S. statement of policy before issuing a declaration. (National Telegram, 2nd)

Key to the Success or Failure of the Conference 67

Will Depend on Hull's Speech Today

(New York) Washington dispatches on President Roosevelt's rejection of the currency stabilization proposal are varied. Some say it is a direct resistance to France, while others say that the President's move is only intended to delay the final decision for a few days so that the dollar can fall to a sufficiently low level to join a private control plan. President Roosevelt's statement that stabilizing currency prices is a banking matter, not a government one, has eliminated hope for stabilizing currency prices unless the Federal Reserve is protected by the U.S. Treasury from losses. The U.S. President believes that permanent stability is hopeless until the gold standard countries have shown their ability to maintain the gold standard. Furthermore, the vague wording of the economic conference's proposals is another reason for the U.S. rejection. The speech of U.S. Chief Delegate Hull on Monday may determine the fate of the conference. (Reuters, 1st)

Yan Huiqing's Pessimism 68

French Newspaper Says the End of the Conference Is Near

(London) Major representatives attending the World Economic Conference, such as Bonnet of France and Colijn of the Netherlands, have mostly returned to their countries. Therefore, the conference has a desolate and quiet atmosphere this morning. Representatives of gold standard countries met this morning but no concrete measures were heard. Representatives from various countries seemed unwilling to openly and practically discuss the issue of adjourning the conference, as they had to wait for the speech of U.S. Chief Delegate Hull on Monday before taking any action. Some sources said that Washington may have suggestions for revising the joint declaration. The only direct criticism of the situation from the gold standard countries this morning came from Dr. Trip, President of the Dutch Bank, who is acting as the chief Dutch delegate during Colijn's absence. It is reported that although President Roosevelt does not agree, the Dutch representatives will continue their gold policy, not only not abandoning it, but also cooperating with other gold standard countries to maintain it. The gold standard countries are deeply aware of the importance of their policy to prevent currency disorder. When asked if the Netherlands was prepared to propose an adjournment, Dr. Trip replied that no rational person could express an opinion on this matter at present. When interviewed by Reuters today, Chinese representative Dr. Yan Huiqing was pessimistic about the situation, saying that in his opinion, from China's standpoint, the gold issue is of utmost importance. If this issue is not resolved, the silver issue cannot be resolved either. French newspapers welcomed the imminent end of the conference with pessimistic remarks. Le Journal Écho de Paris said that the economic conference no longer has a reason to exist. (Reuters, 2nd)

France Uses Adjournment as Leverage 69

While Trying to Win Over Britain

Britain Does Not Believe the Conference Will Break Down

(London) Representatives from various countries in London have reported the news of the U.S. President's rejection of the currency stabilization proposal to their respective governments. It is heard that the American side here believes that the proposal must be redrafted before the U.S. President can accept it. President Roosevelt telegraphed the U.S. delegation in London last night, without mentioning any agreement on central bank cooperation. The U.S. President believes that there can be no permanent stability until all countries are on a permanent monetary basis. There is a serious movement in France advocating adjournment of the conference, unwilling to continue empty talk that only benefits market speculation. It is heard that French Prime Minister Daladier holds this view. According to French sources, Professor Moley, who recently arrived in England from the U.S. representing the U.S. President, clearly warned the U.S. President that if the U.S. does not join the joint declaration on stabilizing currency prices, it will result in the adjournment of the conference. Opposition newspapers pointed out that President Roosevelt is very similar to Robinson Crusoe living alone on a desert island. British officials are unwilling to criticize the U.S. President's attitude but do not acknowledge the claim that the economic conference is about to break down. (Reuters, 1st)

(London) The French side at the World Economic Conference stated that even if President Roosevelt does not approve of any form of joint declaration, France does not want to withdraw from the conference. However, France's belief that the conference can achieve important achievements will be completely destroyed. The French believe that the future of the conference lies with Britain. If the U.S. President is unwilling to issue a joint declaration, then Britain should make closer contact with the European bloc. (Reuters, 1st)

Fate of the Gold Standard 70

Depends on Currency Stabilization Measures

(New York) The general public in the U.S. believes that if currency stabilization cannot be achieved quickly, the Netherlands will abandon the gold standard after eight days, and Switzerland, Belgium, and France will follow suit in the short term. (Havas, 1st) (London) Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain said in a speech at a Conservative Party meeting that it may be difficult to achieve uniform currency stabilization among countries at present, and that current currency speculation, which causes prices to fluctuate erratically, only increases the difficulty. All countries concerned must at least stop this. (Havas, 1st)

Even Without Gold, Will Never Abandon the Gold Standard

Criticizes the Conference for Not Addressing Debt Issues

(Berlin) President Schacht of the German National Bank told reporters here this morning that Britain and the U.S. are using purely unilateral means to lower the price of their currencies, hindering Germany's competition in the world market. Gold standard countries should cooperate with each other to resist Britain and the U.S. Germany, although without gold, is determined not to abandon the gold standard. Schacht also criticized the World Economic Conference for not addressing debt issues. (Reuters, 1st)

Stock Prices Rise by Three Pounds Sterling

(New York) New York stock prices rose again this morning by one to three pounds sterling, due to the excitement caused by hearing President Roosevelt's statement that the dollar exchange rate has not fallen to a sufficiently low level. Although there was news that central banks of various countries would conclude an agreement for international efforts, trading remained high as the dollar fell. Business Weekly published an editorial entitled "The Spectacle of Inflation Business Based Solely on Confidence," stating that the U.S. government has not implemented a true inflation policy, that the currency in circulation has decreased by 180 million yuan since March, that bank lending to the industrial sector has not expanded, and that the Federal Reserve Bank has not exercised its temporary contingency power to inject government debt into banks. Australia Restricts Wheat 73

Sydney The Australian Federal Prime Ministers met in secret today to discuss the issue of reducing wheat fields and have reportedly agreed on a satisfactory solution. The Australian Central Cabinet will consider it and then telegraph the Australian representatives in London. The Cabinet is scheduled to meet tomorrow to consider the Australian representatives' reply. It is reported that those in charge said that the Federal Prime Ministers have agreed to the restriction of wheat exports. (Reuters, 1st)

(London) There is indeed hope for an agreement on the wheat issue at the World Economic Conference today. The Australian representatives received a telegram from the Australian government containing the resolutions of the Federal Prime Ministers' meeting and the Australian government's instructions. It is said that the main issues of finance and economics should be resolved first, followed by wheat and other matters. However, Australia acknowledges in principle the temporary measures for restricting wheat exports, provided that Australian interests are not discriminated against and that European wheat producers also cooperate effectively in this plan. The Federal Prime Ministers agreed on a principle that, in view of the world's existing surplus, Australia should not store more wheat than its usual needs in the next two years. (Reuters, 2nd)

Inside Story of U.S. Attitude 74

To Implement Currency Stabilization Slowly

To Wait for Prices to Gradually Increase

(Washington) Roosevelt sent banker Baruch to England as his liaison with the U.S. delegation to the economic conference. Baruch plans to depart eastward on July 15, directly to France. Baruch claims that his trip has nothing to do with the London conference, but he may consult with leaders of the U.S. delegation in Europe. Roosevelt, aboard the cruiser "Indianapolis," will arrive at Annapolis and has telegraphed various ministers and senior government officials to go there on Monday to discuss currency stabilization and other issues. Roosevelt is scheduled to return to Washington on Tuesday. All plans to inspect naval bases in Guantanamo, Cuba, Puerto Rico, and the Panama Canal defense works will be postponed. Roosevelt's reason for rejecting the European currency stabilization plan is actually due to concerns about the views of the inflation faction, which occupies a majority in Congress. This faction wants Roosevelt to use the currency inflation privileges granted by Congress to raise prices, at least to the level of 1926. The general public mostly agrees with stabilizing the dollar at 70 cents, but they fear that it will hinder the price policy, so they do not want to make a hasty decision. Some quarters are encouraging Roosevelt to seek to have all countries abandon the gold standard, and then stabilize currencies based on the actual status of each country and according to the needs of international commerce. In short, Roosevelt's opinions are also inconsistent, but they all believe that the U.S. has not abandoned the currency stabilization plan, but will implement it slowly. (Havas, 1st)

U.S. New Foreign Policy 78

(Washington) According to those familiar with U.S. political affairs, the U.S.'s new foreign policy can be summarized as follows: ㈠ The U.S. believes that the disarmament conference will eventually fail, so it has decided to abandon its wait-and-see attitude and focus on consolidating its national defense. It will soon begin a three-year naval construction plan, building 32 warships and 290 aircraft, while establishing four naval bases, two each on the Pacific and Atlantic coasts. ㈡ The U.S. has suggested to Europe that it establish a consultation treaty to guarantee peace, but Europe has not followed the U.S.'s lead. The U.S. is now preparing to notify European countries that if they do not listen to the U.S., the U.S. will let them be and will no longer interfere in European affairs. ㈢ Regarding the international economic conference, the U.S. focuses first on ensuring the happiness of the American people. This is true for tariffs and currency issues, as well as for war debts. Therefore, the U.S. will reject debt countries' requests for concessions that would increase the burden on U.S. taxpayers. U.S. political circles acknowledge that this new foreign policy trend is absolutely contradictory to the principles announced by the Roosevelt government in recent months and believe that this new policy will cause a reversal in the entire world politics. (Havas, 1st)

Severe Flood Losses of Five to Six Million Yuan in Various Parts of Korea 83

Japanese United Press Dispatch, Seoul, 2nd - The Police Bureau of the Korean Governor-General's Office announced on the 1st regarding the flood incidents in various parts of Korea that, according to reports received by the Police Bureau on the afternoon of the 1st, heavy rains fell across Korea, causing floods everywhere, even greater than those of the 14th year of the Taisho era. Traffic was cut off in various places. The currently ascertained damage includes 19 deaths, 7 injuries, more than 10 missing persons, over 100 houses washed away, and 4,600 houses submerged. The tracks of the Central Railway were washed away, and traffic was completely cut off. The area downstream of the Nakdong River is currently the most dangerous. The Chinhae Naval Base has dispatched rescue ships, and the fire brigade and youth corps are fully mobilized for vigilance. The state of damage in the southern part of Korea is unknown, but the loss of agricultural products seems to be very large. The loss of roads, bridges, communication facilities, etc., is no less than five to six million yuan.

Floodwaters Recede in Wuhan 86

Dikes and Sluices Near the Suburbs Are Safe

Various Counties Report Disasters in Succession

Hankou Correspondence - Until the 25th of last month, the waters of the Yangtze River in Wuhan fortunately did not continue to rise. The 26th, 27th, and 28th were stable, and the water began to recede on the 29th, dropping from the highest water level of 47.2 feet to 47 feet. From the 30th to the 1st of this month, it continued to recede by 2 inches each day, reaching a water mark of 46.6 feet. The riverbank has now reached the level of the plains. Superficially, it seems that the dangerous period has passed. However, the dikes and sluices near the suburbs still need repair, and disaster reports are pouring in from various counties. The return of the rainy season is imminent, and the level of danger may be several times greater than this time.

During the highest water level this time, the dikes and sluices near Wuhan were mostly in a precarious state. In addition to the Jinshui New Dam in Wuchang and the Xinhewan in Hanyang, which had collapsed one after another, the Wutai Sluice, Wufeng Dike, Wujin Dike, Wuhui Dike, Wuqing Sluice, Baishazhou Dike, Xujiapeng Dike, and Zhoujiazuizi Sluice in Wuchang all reported leaks. After the Flood Prevention Committee worked hard to repair them, they are now safe. However, the embankments of the riverside roads have been eroded and submerged in water for a long time, causing the soil and stones to seep and collapse suddenly. The losses are not very heavy. In order to prevent the return of the rainy season, the Flood Prevention Committee is still working intensely, resolving to repair all the dikes while the river water recedes. On the 1st, it organized nine engineering teams, each with 500 workers, and divided them into four sections to construct repairs. The first section is from Jinkou to Baiguan, the second section is the Wutai Sluice, the third section is Xiaxinhe, and the fourth section is the Wufeng Dike, spanning hundreds of miles. It is planned to complete all of them simultaneously within the shortest possible time. In Hankou, more than 300 cracks appeared in the riverside flood prevention dikes and 43 sluice gates and 13 culvert gates were blocked by the municipal government. Leaks were found at the Zhanggong Dike, the Daijiashan Sluice Gate, and the Liuhegou Wharf, as well as leaks at Fenjinlu and Chenjiaji. The Changfeng Dike has the lowest terrain and is particularly dangerous, but it has also been rescued separately by the municipal government, filled in, and thickened, and it seems that it has also escaped danger.

As for the various counties, they are still reporting disasters in succession. In addition to the 17 places counted by the provincial government, several more have recently been added. 1) Fankou: The entire town is submerged in water, and all the villages have become wetlands. The dikes and sluices are full of crevices and are in a precarious state. The dikes and sluices there are entrusted with the lives and property of the four counties of Wuchang, Daye, Huanggang, and Echeng, and the relationship is the most important. 2) Xindi: The entire city was flooded, and the main dikes along the river for eighty miles are on the verge of collapse. The areas of Luoshan and Tieniutang are particularly dangerous. 3) Songzi: The flooded area is very wide, and the disaster is very serious. 4) Shishou: More than fifty zhang of the Maocaoling Tanaojiang embankment collapsed, and more than 4,000 mu of farmland were flooded. The General Headquarters is paying special attention to the dangerous projects in various places. On the 1st, it issued orders to the troops stationed in various places, requesting them to assist the local flood prevention and rescue efforts as much as possible. It ordered the Jianghan Engineering Bureau to formulate a plan and first contact the local garrison and county magistrate to avoid feeling difficulties in times of emergency. It also ordered the county governments to fulfill their responsibilities regarding the conscription of labor and materials and not to shirk their responsibilities in the slightest. If there is any failure in implementation, they will be severely punished. At the same time, the Engineering Office of the National Economic Commission appointed Zhang Chongji as the special inspector of the Xiangjiang Dike, Gao Lingmei as the special inspector of the upper reaches of the Yangtze River, Tang Shangsong as the special inspector of the lower reaches of the Yangtze River, Cheng Renwu as the special inspector of Wuhan, and Lei Zhongyun as the flood prevention engineer of Wuhan. They will set off separately today, and the eight simple rules for the inspection of the Jianghan dike project are stipulated as follows: 1) In order to strictly protect the main dikes of Jianghan, the main dikes of Jianghan will be divided into three areas during the flood season, and one special inspector will be set up in each area. 2) The sections of the first and second engineering offices below Hankou are the lower district of Hankou, the sections of the third and fourth engineering offices above Hankou and the Xindi engineering office are the upper district of Hankou, and the sections of the fifth and sixth engineering offices and the Shayang third engineering office in the Xiang River basin are the Xiang River district. 3) The special inspectors shall abide by various flood prevention regulations, inspect each dike at any time, and urge all levels of personnel in each engineering office to protect them carefully day and night. If there are special merits or negligence that causes errors, they shall truthfully report them for verification and handling. 4) The special inspectors shall obtain the daily water level of each sub-station of each engineering office and the progress report of all flood prevention work every day, and report it once every ten days. If there are special circumstances, they shall also send separate telegrams at any time. 5) The various charts and forms required by the special inspectors shall be borrowed from the Jianghan Engineering Bureau nearby. 6) The special inspectors may transfer one clerk or secretary from the Jianghan Engineering Bureau to handle all affairs. 7) The travel expenses required by the special inspectors shall be reported according to the travel expense regulations of the association and paid from the flood prevention fee. 8) These simple rules shall be implemented from the date of approval (1st).

Shandong Provincial Government Takes Over the Jinan Arsenal 89

Renamed the Ordnance Bureau and Has Been Taken Over

Will Also Manufacture Agricultural and Industrial Machinery in the Future

Jinan Correspondence - The Jinan Arsenal of the Ministry of Military Affairs has now been transferred to the Shandong Provincial Government for management. Jiang Shaochang, a military counselor of the Ministry of Military Affairs, Liu Shouyu, a member of the Ordnance Bureau, Tang Xiang, the director of the Shandong Provincial Government's office in Beijing, Wang Xuezhi, the director of the Ordnance Bureau, and Hu Tianyi, the director of the factory, have completed the handover procedures. The Jinan Arsenal was renamed the Jinan Ordnance Bureau, and the handover was implemented this morning (1st). Han Fuju, the chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government, appointed Wang Xuezhi, the director of the 3rd Ordnance Bureau, as the director of the Jinan Ordnance Bureau and went to take over. Hu Tianyi, the former director of the factory, ordered his department heads to be responsible for the handover. Because there are many parts in the factory, the inventory was not completed until the afternoon. The reporter learned that the factory has more than 1,500 workers and is one of the few arsenals in North China. I specially visited Wang Xuezhi to ask about the current situation of the factory, the handover process, and the future rectification plan. I am grateful to report them one by one as follows:

Current Status of the Factory 90

According to Wang, the factory is divided into three major departments: machinery, bombs, and bullets, with more than 1,500 workers. The administrative aspect is divided into three departments: general affairs, engineering, and inspection, and there is also an audit section. Unless there are special manufacturing expenses, the monthly labor and material costs are about 150,000 yuan. In recent days, he has been negotiating with Director Hu, Counselor Jiang, and Member Liu about the handover methods. The main points are that all old products will be transported to Beijing, and the existing materials will be fairly valued by the Ordnance Bureau after the inventory is completed, and the price will be paid. The inventory has not yet been completed and cannot be valued. However, the official seal documents have not been handed over. Our side has organized a takeover committee. Yu is the chairman of the committee, and Zhang Jincheng, Shi Enxian, Zhang Chengyuan, Liu Zixiang, Li Hanzhang, Zhang Chunting, Song Enxin, the section chiefs of the Ordnance Bureau, and a certain member of the military medical office are members, responsible for the takeover. It will probably take two or three months to complete. Work has now been suspended and will resume on the 3rd. Also, Member Liu of the Ministry of Military Affairs came to the bureau today to inspect.

Rectification Plan 91

It is also said that Chairman Han's purpose in taking over this factory is to maintain the lives of more than 1,500 workers and their families of 5,000 to 6,000 people, and to manufacture bullets for the needs of the province's army and the militia groups of various counties for reserve. In the future, the rectification plan will be: First, the machinery factory will be reorganized to manufacture products. In addition to military supplies, it is also planned to manufacture machinery needed for agriculture and industry in order to resist foreign goods, recover rights and interests, and help rural areas. It is expected that the Ordnance Bureau will also serve as the Agricultural and Industrial Bureau. Because the current machinery factory can only repair machines but cannot manufacture products, the cost will be reduced as much as possible in the future to avoid waste. It is not yet certain whether the 3rd Ordnance Bureau will be merged here. If the central government needs supplies, this bureau should still provide them as usual as much as possible, because it is a temporary Shandong operation and not taken as its own, he also said (1st).

Wuxi

Han Wentai's Torn Ticket and Corpse Retrieval 94

Han Wentai, the head of Zhouxin Town, Xiexie Township, in the third district (Yangming Township) of the county, was robbed by more than a dozen bandits on the night of March 20th of this year. When they left, they kidnapped Han Wentai. Afterwards, the bandits repeatedly sent letters demanding a huge sum of more than 10,000 yuan. After Han's family repeatedly sent people to contact the bandits, the result was that the bandits had to extort a minimum of 8,000 yuan before allowing the ticket to be redeemed. The Han family tried every means to raise 2,400 yuan in cash, and entrusted someone to contact the bandits and hand over the money to the bandits. However, because the bandits obtained too little money, they still hid the ticket in the bandit den. Recently, the Criminal Investigation Team of the Public Security Bureau captured four bandits involved in the kidnapping and transferred them to the county government for interrogation and detention. Now, it is learned that County Magistrate Yan of the county government also paid great attention to the case. Although he secretly ordered his subordinates to tighten the search for the remaining bandits and rescue the ticket, he could not find any clues. Therefore, the county case has not yet rescued the ticket. The day before yesterday, County Magistrate Yan suddenly received a secret report stating that the ticket bandit Yang A-bao (i.e., Zhou A-bao) was hiding in Zhoujiage above Zhangjingqiao, three miles away in the seventh district, and asked to send the police to arrest him as soon as possible. After receiving the report, County Magistrate Yan secretly ordered Wu Zhengrong, the political police chief, to find a way to arrest him. After receiving the order, Police Chief Wu led all the political police on a gasoline boat to the countryside to arrest him at about 6:00 AM yesterday (2nd). Yang A-bao was captured on the spot, and under strict interrogation, the bandit directly admitted to watching the ticket. The ticket, Han Wentai, was hidden in my house. He has now been torn up for about a month. The corpse is buried in a wild animal cave in the Gan Ke wilderness on He Feng near Zhang Wei. After obtaining the confession, Police Chief Wu led the bandit to the burial site to excavate, and indeed obtained Han Wentai's corpse, which had rotted and had no coffin. The most pitiful thing was that the corpse was actually cut into four pieces. He ordered the chief Chen Xiangsheng to be responsible for guarding. At the same time, Cheng Xu, the captain of the second police squadron stationed in Zhangjingqiao, also sent two patrol officers to assist in watching the corpse. The bandit Yang A-bao, who had been captured, was escorted to the city by Police Chief Wu and sent to the county government. The court was interrogated by clerk Yao, and he was ordered to be detained. A notice was sent to Han's family to go to identify the corpse, and Chief Chen Xiangsheng was scheduled to report to the county court for inspection today together with the corpse's family.

Zhenjiang

Water Stove Businesses Resume Operations 96

The water stove case in the provincial capital, involving the water company's price increase, resulted in a unanimous strike. Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, a petition was submitted to the county party headquarters, which immediately convened its 58th committee meeting, with Shi Shunyuan, the training section chief from the provincial party headquarters, in attendance. It is reported that four resolutions were made regarding the water stove industry's dispute with the water company over price increases: 1) The water price for water stove businesses will be calculated at 90% of the adjusted price after mediation. 2) Water fee deposits and water meter deposit cabinets will be paid in installments. 3) If a water stove business does not operate for three days, the Public Security Bureau may revoke its business license and will notify the Public Security Bureau accordingly. 4) The water company shall not force any water stove business to use water if they are unwilling to bear the water price in the first resolution. The county party headquarters will dispatch Committee Member Xu Luan to respond. It is reported that all water stove businesses consider this satisfactory and will resume operations tomorrow.

Wang Jingwei Flew to Shanghai the Day Before Yesterday, Returned to Nanjing Last Night 107

Thirty Hours in Shanghai

His whereabouts were extremely secretive

He then took a car to the North Station last night and boarded the night express train to Nanjing. Those traveling with him included Chu Minyi, Yang Dezhao, Zou Lin, and others.

Wang's visit to Shanghai this time was extremely secretive. Our reporter received a telegram from Nanjing the day before yesterday, learning that Wang had indeed flown to Shanghai with Zeng Zhongming. That evening, he went to Wang's residence on Pushi Road to inquire. Wang's family denied this, saying that Wang was still in Nanjing and had not come. He then went to various related places, but could not obtain any information and was unable to confirm Wang's arrival in Shanghai. Yesterday morning, our reporter went to Wang's residence again to inquire. According to Wang's secretary, Lin Ruyan, Wang and Vice Minister Zeng did indeed arrive in Shanghai by plane at around 3:00 PM yesterday (July 1st) and went to Noel Hospital to treat his back paralysis. Last night (July 1st) at 11:00 PM, they had already taken a train from Zhenru Station back to Nanjing, and his wife, Ms. Chen Bijun, and Tieci Zeng Zhongming did not travel with him. After Wang left Nanjing the day before yesterday, there were conflicting reports about whether he flew to Shanghai or Ganzhou. Only now has the truth come to light.

Sun Ke Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Morning 108

Talked Freely About the Recent Political Situation

Central News Agency reports: Sun Ke, the President of the Legislative Yuan, arrived in Shanghai last night on the night train from Nanjing. He arrived at the North Station at around 8:00 AM yesterday morning and immediately returned to his residence to rest. A Central News Agency reporter visited Mr. Sun at his private residence yesterday morning and inquired about various issues, such as the new customs import tariff. He provided the following detailed answers:

New Customs Tariff 109

According to Mr. Sun, the new customs import tariff was drafted by the Ministry of Finance, submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval, and then submitted to the Central Political Council for review. The Central Political Council considered this tariff to be of great importance. If it were leaked, merchants would know which items would be subject to increased taxes and by how much, and would order and ship goods to China in advance to avoid the tax increase, leading to significant abuses. Therefore, it was decided to first announce and implement the tariff, and then submit it to the Legislative Yuan for review and amendment. Once the amendment is completed, it will be announced again and implemented according to the revised tariff. The Legislative Yuan is currently working on the review, based on the principle of protecting customs revenue. The import tax rate for luxury goods will be increased. For necessities, such as paper, etc., which can be manufactured domestically but are in short supply, the original tax rate will be maintained without increase. Other items that can be manufactured domestically and do not need to be imported will also be slightly increased. However, there will be very few revisions, and it will be completed soon. As for the dumping tariff, it has not yet been submitted to the Legislative Yuan for review.

Xinjiang Aftermath 110

Turning to the Xinjiang incident, Mr. Sun said that since Special Envoy Huang arrived in Xinjiang to convey the central government's intentions and appease the people, the situation has eased. Various ministries, provinces, and armies have united and defeated Ma Zhongying's army. The government is currently studying the handling of the aftermath. In terms of politics, the provincial government must be reorganized to promote political reform. However, the candidates have not yet been decided. Special Envoy Huang may be appointed as the chairman, or someone else may be appointed. In terms of military affairs, because the provincial armies have not cooperated in the past, they must also be reorganized. Sheng Shicai's troops have made the most efforts to maintain local order. Therefore, after the reorganization of the provincial armies, they may be under his command. The central government has also dispatched troops to jointly maintain security. As for the Northeast Anti-Japanese troops who retreated to Russia and then entered Xinjiang, such as Ma Su and Li's troops, there is no specific plan on how to deal with them. The above issues are relatively easy to resolve. What is considered difficult is the province's finances. Because there are no banks established there, the provincial government has issued paper money in excess, amounting to 150 million taels, while the market price is only three cents per tael, with a total value of only about 4 million taels. Therefore, the finances are chaotic and the finances are difficult. The government plans to establish a branch of the Central Bank in the province to reorganize it. This proposal is also under study.

Opinions on Sichuan Affairs 111

Mr. Sun went on to say that the rumor that Sichuan Reconstruction Director Liu Xiang borrowed 30 million yuan from Britain was completely untrue. Given the current global economic downturn, this huge loan is impossible, and the solution to the Sichuan problem cannot be achieved simply by borrowing money. Mr. Sun also expressed his views on the matter, saying that the reform of provincial administration lies in the ability of the military leaders to work together in harmony. On the negative side, they should jointly suppress bandits to alleviate the people's suffering and reduce the people's burden. On the positive side, they should strive for construction to restore local vitality. Currently, the armies are not thinking about this, but are competing for personal territory, causing internal strife, wasting resources, and harassing the people, which is extremely harmful and gives the Communists an opportunity to cause trouble. Therefore, if the leaders do not realize this, there will be no hope of clearing up and reforming the provincial administration.

Fifth National Congress 112

The candidates for representatives from various regions for the Fifth National Congress have been selected, and overseas representatives have returned to the country to report. It is expected that the meeting will be held as scheduled. Zhang Xueliang is about to leave London and return to Rome for recuperation. There is no news of his return to the country. Regarding the American cotton and wheat loan, Mr. Hu Zhantang sent two telegrams opposing it, which have been published in the newspapers. Since this matter has become a fact, I replied with an explanation, fearing that it would cause misunderstanding and resentment, so I did not reply.

If any comrades wish to revise their province's duties, they may take advantage of this leisure time to return to their hometowns. However, they must remain consistent in their anti-Japanese work and persevere to the end. Do not be distracted by prosperity and disturb your minds. The dead are gone, the living can make a difference. As long as there is a breath left, this determination will not waver. I hope to share this with all comrades." He then discussed settlement plans with his subordinates, including the distribution of travel expenses and all post-settlement issues. The discussion lasted for about an hour before it ended.

Araki Fears Our International Aviation 129

Accusing it of being an illegal movement

And intending to find ways to suppress it

The Tokyo Hochi Shimbun reported on June 28th that Army Minister Araki, at the regular cabinet meeting on the 27th, reported on the China issue, requesting that all cabinet members pay special attention. He stated that, according to recently obtained intelligence, the Nanjing government is establishing a large-scale air route between Shanghai and Berlin, and between Shanghai and Moscow, with Shanghai as the center. This will soon be realized. If this large-scale new air route appears, it will have a significant impact on military affairs in the Far East. In recent years, illegal movements have increasingly become internationalized. Therefore, the suppression of this type of construction is considered extremely important. Following Araki's report, the cabinet members requested the Ministry of Interior, in conjunction with relevant ministries, to immediately begin an investigation to devise a unified countermeasure.

After the communication, a directive was received stating that, considering the special circumstances of silk factories having their own water supply equipment, and to show consideration for the difficulties of businesses, a flexible approach will be adopted. Five accounting procedures are to be registered within a specified period. In addition to the association notifying the silk factories, it is requested that all representatives pay attention. ㈤ District committee members reported on the operation of silk reeling machines in their respective districts after the arrival of new cocoons.

Resolutions of various proposals: ㈠ Unified treatment methods for various silk factories: Resolved, to seek legal solutions through Party and government organs. ㈡ Decision on the association fees for this year: Resolved, to collect association fees this year at a rate of 5 jiao per silk reeling machine per year, to be paid in one lump sum. ㈢ Proposal on how to handle the matter of various silk factories requesting the Transfer, Consolidation, and Preservation Committees to rescind the subsidization of excess exports of silk and to not issue public bonds accordingly: Resolved, to request the three committees to rescind the original resolution and to handle the matter in accordance with the subsidy methods announced by the executive and legislative branches. ㈣ Proposal on increasing wages and changing methods: Resolved, to wait for Party and government organs to convene discussions to find a solution.

Letters from various silk factories: Eighteen silk factories from Jiangsu and Zhejiang, including Yuanji, Yuanxing, Baotai, Yuanxin, Hongsheng, and Fukang, have not yet received government public bond subsidies for 614 bales of Chen-era silk, making it impossible to load and export them. Therefore, at yesterday's extraordinary general meeting of representatives, it was resolved to send a letter to the Preservation, Consolidation, and Transfer Committees, questioning the reasons why these committees violated the original proposal of the Legislative and Executive Yuans to issue short-term public bonds for the silk industry of Jiangsu and Zhejiang in the 22nd year of the Republic (1933), and for arbitrarily changing the distribution methods for subsidizing the export costs of Chen-era silk from the Jiangsu and Zhejiang provincial governments. The original letter stated: "To the esteemed sirs, we have received government consideration for the decline of the silk industry, issuing three million yuan in short-term public bonds for the silk industry of Jiangsu and Zhejiang in the 21st year of the Republic (1932), subsidizing the export of Chen-era silk from Jiangsu and Zhejiang, stipulating the end of May of this year as the deadline for subsidies. It is now known that the number of silk exported within the deadline is 20,614 bales in total. On the 23rd of this month, a joint meeting of the Consolidation Committee, the Transfer Committee, and the Fund Committee intends to allocate the surplus from the expenses of 7 yuan per bale of silk paid by silk merchants to the Transfer and Consolidation Committees to subsidize the export of another 614 bales of silk. The reasons for this are truly perplexing. If the committees have such a resolution, it is an illegal action, and the factories absolutely cannot recognize it. We respectfully offer the following reasons based on facts: ㈠ The Legislative Yuan passed the Public Bond Regulations, and the Executive Yuan announced the principles for subsidizing Chen-era silk from Jiangsu and Zhejiang, issuing a total of 3 million yuan in public bonds, with 140 yuan in public bonds subsidized per bale of silk. There are no other supplementary explanations or detailed rules. ㈡ The current number of silk exported is 20,614 bales, for which public bonds should be issued totaling 2,885,960 yuan. There is still a surplus according to the approved public bonds. ㈢ Since the public bonds have regulations, they should be strictly followed. The regulations stipulate that they are specifically for subsidizing the silk industry and should not be diverted for other uses. ㈣ The silk merchants have paid expenses to the Transfer and Consolidation Committees, and if there is a surplus in the reserve fund, it should be returned to the silk merchants. Even if we take a step back, it should be given to the silk merchants' group for use in the silk industry. However, the committees disregard the original proposal of the Legislative Yuan and the government's decrees, arbitrarily moving the surplus funds from the reserve expenses paid by the silk merchants and making a hasty resolution that we cannot recognize. Therefore, we jointly request your esteemed committee to immediately raise an objection to these committees, requesting the rescission of the resolution, and to submit a statement to the Ministry of Industry and the Ministry of Finance, as well as the governments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, stating the reasons for non-recognition. We beg for your assistance and request that you proceed in accordance with the Administrative Appeal Law to show great trust and to benefit the public. Respectfully addressed to the Shanghai Silk Factory Trade Association Committee."

City Chamber of Commerce Petitions Legislative Yuan to Revise Joint and Several Liability for Partnerships 131

Advocating the maintenance of the custom of proportionate sharing of liabilities

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, based on the resolution of the fourth session of member representatives, petitioned the Legislative Yuan yesterday to revise the joint and several liability for partnerships. The original text stated, "Petition for a request: The Chamber held its fourth member general meeting on June 25th. According to the proposals submitted by the six trade associations of Grains, Oil Cakes, Bean Noodles, Wheat Bran, Grains and Cotton, Rice Milling, and Timber, 'We believe that in our country's business organizations, except for the new-style enterprises in major trading ports, which occasionally adopt the company system, most ordinary businesses still use the partnership system. These types of partnership organizations account for the absolute majority in the business community, and their history is also the longest. The conditions for their organization must first be mutually agreed upon. This agreement is a valid contract. All rights and obligations regarding each partner's subscribed share and the sharing of profits and losses are clearly stated. The allocation of responsibility for external debts in the future is based on this agreement. If any partner has insufficient assets to pay off debts, the other partners are only responsible for the shares they hold. This unchangeable custom has become a common practice in the business world. Since the promulgation and implementation of the Civil Law Debt Compilation Enforcement Law on May 5th, the 19th year of the Republic (1930), the regulations regarding partnerships, namely Article 681 of the Civil Law, state that when the partnership property is insufficient to pay off the partnership's debts, each partner is jointly and severally liable for the deficiency. The original intention of the legislative authorities was to protect creditor rights. However, while protecting creditor rights, consideration should also be given to the debtor's situation to achieve fairness and justice. The establishment of such legal provisions completely disregards the inherent practices of commerce and the original customs of partnership operations. This forces partners to bear extra losses of joint and several liability due to the failure of a portion of the business, or even face the danger of sacrificing all their assets. This is unfair. Moreover, partners only enjoy the right to share profits in proportion to their shares, but bear joint and several liability for external debts. Considering the meaning of the reciprocal relationship between rights and obligations, it does not seem appropriate. Taking Shanghai as an example, cases formed due to the aforementioned legal provisions have emerged one after another. The old partnership organizations are urgently seeking dissolution, and new organizations are disappearing from the market. Who would dare to try again after weighing the pros and cons? From then on, the organization of partnership businesses will become a past relic in history. This strict legal restriction is no less than blocking the opportunity for individual economic development. It is not only greatly related to the rise and fall of commerce but also has a great impact on the entire social economy. Our Chamber cannot ignore the situation we have witnessed. We dare to jointly petition your esteemed Chamber to gather public opinion and maintain commerce, and to forward this to the government and the executive, legislative, and judicial branches. Please propose to amend Article 681 of the Civil Law as soon as possible to determine that partnership debts are shared in proportion to shares, without joint and several liability, and to maintain the inherent customs to conform to the freedom of contract. Otherwise, temporarily suspend the application of the aforementioned legal provisions until the Civil Law is amended in the future. All merchants in the country will rely on this. Is this appropriate? We respectfully await your public decision.' It was found that this matter was submitted by the Chamber to your esteemed Yuan on March 10th.

We requested that your esteemed Yuan amend the item in question, on the grounds that the national legislative policy should protect both creditors and debtors, according to the principle of joint protection, with debts shared in proportion to shares, ultimately settled with a discount if there are insufficient funds to repay. This is a common practice in our country's business community. Creditors' investments are not necessarily concentrated in one store. Even if debts are repaid at a discount, it is the same as having a discount in trade, and there is no danger of bankruptcy. If debtors are held jointly and severally liable, creditors must recover their principal and interest in full. In this situation, partners may not be able to repay even if they go bankrupt. This kind of European and American characteristic that uniquely favors the creditor and uniquely cruelly treats the debtor does not conform to our country's spirit of fairness and forgiveness. If this example prevails, why would investors not invest in land and housing instead of partnering to do business? Even if there is a danger of fluctuations in land value, at most they would lose their land and housing, and would not go completely bankrupt and be involved in endless troubles. This kind of policy is only enough to guide cash to concentrate in the city and hinder the development of industry and commerce. From the merchants' point of view, there are lenders and borrowers. Creditor and debtor are not like two completely separate entities. This argument is not to reduce one's own responsibility but to seek fairness in legislative policy. Subsequently, on March 23rd, we received a reply from the Secretariat of your esteemed Yuan, stating that it had been instructed to refer to the Civil Law Committee for reference. The revision is still a distant prospect. The impact on commerce is not minor. After being submitted to the General Assembly for a vote, it was resolved to be passed and submitted to the Legislative Yuan for revision on file. It is appropriate to record the case and present it for your esteemed Yuan's review, and to approve its implementation. Respectfully presented to the Legislative Yuan."

Yang Xingfo Was Buried Yesterday 132

Cai Yuanpei Personally Assisted with the Coffin

Wu Zhihui's Old Tears Wanted to Fall

Zhao Zhidao Swallowed Her Grief in Silence

The late Yang Xingfo, executive director of the Academia Sinica, was mourned at the Universal Funeral Home yesterday morning. Kong Xiangxi also went to pay respects. The funeral procession set off at 3 PM in the afternoon, and Wu Zhihui and others also assisted with the coffin. All the relatives and friends mourned with tears. The details are divided into the following:

Visitors 133

Before Yang's funeral procession yesterday, those who went to the Universal Funeral Home on Jiaozhou Road to offer condolences were endless. Executive Yuan President Wang Jingwei (represented by Chu Minyi), Central Bank Governor Kong Xiangxi, Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng (represented by Yu Hongjun), Central Committee Members Wu Zhihui and He Xiangning, Academia Sinica President Cai Yuanpei, Central Political Committee Secretary-General Tang Youren, Executive Yuan Secretary-General Chu Minyi, Executive Yuan Political Affairs Director Peng Xuepei, Municipal Government Secretary-General Yu Hongjun, Supervisory Committee Member Gao Lu, Legislative Committee Member Xie Shoukang, Jiaotong University President Li Zhaohuan, Jinan University President Zheng Hongnian, Salt Revenue Audit Office Director Xie Qi, City Chamber of Commerce Chairman Wang Xiaolai, as well as Zhang Shouyong, Ou Yuanhuai, Chen Hexian, Yan Fuqing, Xu Xinliu, Hu Gangfu, Xue Dubi, Cai Wuji, Zhuang Zhihuan, Guo Dehua, Zhang Weici, Wang Yunwu, Shen Junru, Lin Yutang, Jiang Xiaojian, Shao Xunmei, Liu Haisu, Li Fuhou, Pan Xulun, Huang Jingwan, and others all went to pay tribute, totaling more than 200 people. Yang's brother Xin, nephew Xianglin, and son Xiaofo stood and knelt in front of the coffin to return the salute.

Yang's coffin being helped onto the hearse by relatives and friends (Photo by Gong Shuxian) 134

Wreaths from Various Parties 135

In addition to those who went to pay tribute in person, Finance Minister Song Ziwen, Industry Minister Chen Gongbo, Communications Minister Zhu Jiahua, Navy Minister Chen Shaokuan, Sun Yat-sen's widow Soong Ching-ling, Health Minister Liu Ruiheng, Central Committee Members Li Shizeng, Chen Mingshu, Li Liejun, Liu Yazi, Nanjing Mayor Shi Ying, Education Deputy Duan Xipeng, Nanjing Garrison Commander Gu Zhenglun, National Central University President Luo Jialun, Peking University President Jiang Menglin, as well as Ye Gongchuo, Wang Jingqi, Yi Peiji, Zhang Zhijiang, Liu Dajun, Xu Shiying, Ma Liang, Fu Sinian, Li Shuhua, Zhou Zuomin, Zou Bingwen, Chen Guangfu, Wu Kaisheng, Chu Fucheng, and Chen Shicen, all sent wreaths and elegiac couplets to express their condolences. Wu Zhihui gave 100 yuan as a gift. The elegiac couplet in the center of the mourning hall was given by his divorced wife, Zhao Zhidao, which read: "Standing among the crowd of snipers, the sound of a falling tree leads to the loss of a gentleman. A single sleep leaves endless sorrow. When will the chaos subside, and the country will be without a day to mourn?" "Considering the two young children in front, I still have the responsibility to raise and care for them. Thousands of times thinking about the past, separation in life brings regret, and farewell in death brings swallowed voices." The upper line read, "Eternal rest for Mr. Yang Xingfo," and the lower line read, "Cried and mourned by Zhao Zhidao."

Funeral Procession 136

The family memorial ceremony was held at noon, with a vegetarian meal offered as a sacrifice. Yang's children and nephews all paid their respects one by one. In the afternoon, many people from all walks of life went to offer condolences. Soon after, the funeral curtains were removed, and the coffin was covered with the flag of the "China Science Society," as Yang was the founder of the society, and a society funeral ceremony was held. At 3 PM, members of the society Wang Jiliang and Hu Gangfu paid their respects in front of the coffin, and then the mourning table was removed. Yang's son Xiaofo, wearing mourning clothes, stood holding the spirit tablet, and members of the society Wang Jiliang, Hu Gangfu, Ding Xunfu, and Zhou Ren helped the coffin onto the prepared hearse. The car was covered with fresh flowers, and Zhao Zhidao's wreath was hung in the front, which read "Eternal rest for Mr. Yang Xingfo" and "Cried and mourned by Zhao Zhidao." The funeral procession set off at 3 PM from the Universal Funeral Home. First, Chinese police opened the way, followed by the hearse. Xiaofo held the spirit seat, and an attendant held Yang's portrait. Third was the coffin car, followed by dozens of cars carrying Cai Yuanpei and others who were seeing off the funeral procession. The procession proceeded from Jiaozhou Road, through Jing'an Temple Road, Jessfield Road, and into Haig Road, through Xujiahui Town, and into Hongqiao Road, and arrived at the Yong'an Cemetery on Robison Road, which was already past 3:30 PM. Kong Xiangxi, Wu Zhihui, Peng Xuepei, Guo Dehua, and others personally assisted with the coffin. The plain carriage and white horse showed all the sorrow and glory of the moment.

Burial Ceremony 137

Yang's coffin was transported to the Yong'an Cemetery and carried down by Wang Jiliang, Hu Gangfu, Ding Xunfu, Zhou Ren and others to place it at the burial site. The coffin was lowered slowly into the ground at 4:00pm. Yang's brothers, sisters, nieces and nephews could not hold back their wails at the moment. Ms. Zhao Zhidao, clad in black cheongsam, was standing silently with unspeakable grief. Yang's relatives and friends were all saddened. Wu Zhihui's tears were about to drop and was unusually mournful. In the midst of this mournful atmosphere, the guests surrounded the graveyard and bowed three times before departing, and the burial ceremony was concluded.

To be Held on July 10 in the Capital

Shanghai Navigation Association to Send Representatives to Attend

Merchant ships of various shipping companies operating on the seas of the four provinces of Shandong, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Guangdong have been repeatedly attacked by pirates.
