Free Talk

On "Examinations" 206

— Zhou Muzhai

In various local examinations, some initially opposed them, while others had examination questions leaked temporarily, causing unrest. The root cause of all this is that the true way of examination was not understood.

There are many ways to conduct examinations. In a nutshell, it is to take the ancient methods as a model. Examination is an ancient method, and the essence of examination is to model the past. Let's examine it. The Shuowen Jiezi says: "Examination means old." This is a rotational definition, so it also says: "Old means examination." "Examination" is interpreted as "old," and "old" is interpreted as "examination," which is still the same thing. We need to think of another way. "Old" refers to adhering to old methods. This is my interpretation. Adhering to old methods means taking the ancient methods as a model. Later generations may say that I am engaging in far-fetched analogies with this kind of exegesis. But in the eyes of teachers and senior scholars, they will definitely sigh and say: "Elucidating the essence and revealing the subtle, Ma Rong and Zheng Xuan have been reborn. Xu Shen has found a kindred spirit, and my way is not alone." I am not boasting, but I am confident, because teachers, senior scholars, and modeling the past are three in one.

Enough small talk, let's get back to the main point. What are the ancient methods of examination? Rewards and punishments, nothing more. The combination of the two is perfect, and the separation of the two is harmful. They must be given equal importance. Intellectuals, whether ancient or modern, high or low, can be attracted with rewards and awed with punishments. When awed with punishments, intellectuals know what to avoid. When attracted with rewards, intellectuals know what to strive for. When the psychology of avoidance and striving merge, examinees will naturally obey examiners like water flows downhill, unstoppable. If only graduation or non-graduation is used as the standard, then graduation is not a reward, and there is no reward for graduation. Non-graduation is not a punishment, and there is no punishment for non-graduation. Therefore, there is no means of control over them, and there is no relationship of restraint. Because there are the same examinations as before, and the same graduation or non-graduation: what distinguishes this kind of examination from that kind of examination?

Old scholars often say that the examinations since the Republic of China only have the dregs of examination, and the essence of examination has been completely lost. The treatment of "epidemics" still requires the use of "ancient prescriptions."

When rituals are lost, we seek them in the countryside. I will offer this as a source of inspiration. Mixing vernacular with literary language, I will seek to integrate them. End of discussion on "examinations."

A Record of Petitioning for the Study of Classics 207

— Cao Juren

In the west, there is a sage who sent a telegram to the whole country, advocating the restoration of classical studies to rectify people's hearts. In the south, there is another sage who proposed a motion, ordering the whole province to study the classics, at least six hours per week, in order to save the declining customs. Rectifying people's hearts and saving declining customs are both great achievements of a prosperous age. The common people respectfully follow the imperial decree and rejoice. They hurriedly put on their straw sandals and went to the west.

Common people: I heard that you are practicing benevolent governance. You are also a sage. I wish to be a subject of the sage.

Western Sage: Good, good, you can go and study the Four Books!

Common people: I don't know if I should study the Four Books after the Song Dynasty or the Four Books before the Song Dynasty?

Western Sage: Huh!

Common people: There were no Four Books before the Song Dynasty (the Great Learning and the Doctrine of the Mean were just two chapters of the Book of Rites). Sage, the Great Learning in the Book of Rites is different from the current Great Learning.

Western Sage: Huh?

Common people: Sage, Cheng Yi said that his version of the Great Learning is good, Zhu Xi said that his version of the Great Learning is the best, and Wang Yangming said that he has an ancient version of the Great Learning to prove it. I don't know which one I should study?

Western Sage: Huh! Even I am confused about this. You don't have to study them.

The common people put on their straw sandals again and sailed south.

Common people: I heard that you are practicing benevolent governance. You are also a sage. I wish to be a subject of the sage.

Southern Sage: Good, good, you can go and study the Five Classics!

Common people: Kang Youwei wants to drag me to study the Gongyang Commentary on the Spring and Autumn Annals. Zhang Taiyan wants to drag me to study the Zuo Commentary on the Spring and Autumn Annals. Huang Yizhou said that the Rites of Zhou is the sage's treasure. Pi Lumen said that studying the Book of Etiquette is the right path. Zhuang Cunyu said that the Book of Poetry should be based on the commentaries of the Qi, Lu, and Han schools. Hui Dingyu told me that I must believe the words of Mao Chang and Zheng Xuan. Which classic should I study?

Southern Sage: Huh? What are you saying?

Common people: Zhuang Cunyu and Liu Fenglu are grabbing Sun Yirang and Huang Yizhou by their queues. Dai Zhen and Gu Yanwu are grabbing Wang Yangming and Lu Jiuyuan by their collars. Zheng Kangcheng is arguing with He Xiu there. Liu Xin slapped the face of a Grand Tutor. Sage, they all have badges of great classics scholars on their bodies!

Southern Sage: Huh, what are you saying?

Common people: Sage, Confucius is angry there. He says: I have never seen any Five Classics or Six Classics, and I have never revised any Five Classics or Six Classics. There must be treacherous people impersonating my name, swindling and deceiving people. Little ones, you can attack them with drums!

Southern Sage: Huh! What are you saying? Even I am confused about this. You don't have to study them!

The common people wholeheartedly wanted to study the classics, but who knew that even the sages didn't know what to study? They had no choice but to put on their straw sandals and return to their hometown. This is precisely:

"Dwarfs watching a play can't see a thing,

They just repeat what others say is short or long!"

Locusts 208

— Sheng Dan

Fufu ran back, his face covered in sweat and oil, and he was furious. He squatted down and sat down, took off his white cloth short shirt that was half draped over his back, threw it onto the bench, frowned, and stared blankly, craning his neck.

"You always look like this, what did the bodhisattva say?" Mama Fufu said, squatting down, shaking Fufu's shoulders with her hands, pursing her shriveled cheeks, and widening her sunken eyes, waiting for his satisfactory answer. However, her chest, which was throbbing, already understood a bit. The "fortune slip" must have been mostly ominous, otherwise, Fufu would not have been so angry. After a while, Fufu threw away his cigarette butt and sighed heavily.

"No! The locusts are going to open their mouths!"

"Who said that?"

"That's what the bodhisattva's 'fortune slip' said!"

Mama Fufu's face suddenly turned white, she pounded her thighs with both hands, and tears streamed down like a string of beads. Then, her throat choked, and she cried out, "My poor Fufu Grandpa!..." Fufu drew on the ground with his fingers, not saying a word.

At this moment, there was a sudden commotion in the field outside. Mama Fufu automatically stopped crying, lifted the corner of her clothes to wipe her eyelids, and went out. She glimpsed the locusts in the sky to the northeast, flying in, covering the sky and the earth. Mama Fufu immediately knelt down and kowtowed dozens of times loudly. It was not until the locusts' large formation had flown over that she stood up trembling, muttering prayers: Mighty General Bodhisattva is efficacious, do not let the divine soldiers eat my rice crops. If the autumn harvest is good this year, I can sell more for a few more dollars. At the same time, she also remembered the locusts four years ago, which also went and returned, and finally ate up two or three hundred acres of rice crops in the surrounding area. It was from that year that the family's situation gradually became difficult, and she began to sell fields, incur debts, and pawn items. Now there were only eight or nine acres of land left. If there was another locust plague, then there would simply be only one way to die. Fufu Grandpa's burial in the winter, Fufu's marriage... These urgent matters that needed to be resolved naturally became even more impossible to hold!

She thought blankly, her eyes reddened, and tears almost burst out again. Fufu lit incense and candles in the hall, respectfully kowtowing and bowing.

One day, two days, five days, although the locusts flew in in groups, they did not open their mouths. Both Mama Fufu and Fufu had some smiles on their faces. All future terrifying fantasies were reduced a lot. Mr. Wang, who was teaching in the village ancestral hall in the back village, said that last night the Mighty General Bodhisattva descended to the altar, "The Divine Soldiers" had already crossed the river and went north, and would definitely not "collect food" in Jiangnan. So when Mama Fufu heard Mr. Wang's stern and resolute words, it seemed like a stone fell from her heart. The neighbors in the whole village also showed a confident look.

Crackle, crackle, crackle!

In the middle of the sixth day, "The Divine Soldiers" suddenly carried out the "food collection." Their battle line extended to more than twenty miles in a few minutes. Mama Fufu knelt straight on the field, her face like a dead person. Fufu ran out bare-chested, then ran back, shouting like crazy:

"It's all gone! Mighty General Bodhisattva!"

In the Carriage 209

— Xu Wei

Inside the carriage, there was only a chaotic, muddled, and boiling cacophony of voices.

With a strange gaze, I sneaked from this side to the end of that side, and then from the end of that side to here. I saw that in this warm, stuffy atmosphere, there were countless complex heads: long, square, round, flat, fat, thin. Each seemed to have lost its soul, moving and shaking aimlessly, just like the uneven waves of wheat ears in autumn, blown by the gentle breeze.

Waves of heads, noisy and continuous, waves of heads, almost made me dizzy.

But just as I lowered my eyelids, a sharp, coughing sound awakened me. I looked on with frightened eyes and heard a "thump." A thick, green, glue-like phlegm jumped from a dark, mysterious mouth with a row of golden teeth onto the carriage floor. The floor seemed to shudder in fear.

I stared blankly at this emerald green phlegm. But just as I was staring blankly, I saw an old, gray-covered shoe blocking my view, as if trying to destroy this phlegm. After a while, it dragged past. The phlegm then turned into a wide, thin white foam.

This white foam looked quietly at the black mouth from which it had just sprung, with a kind of terrible smile. At this time, the black mouth seemed to be returning its smile and slowly opened wider. But then, a dirty hand, holding a snow-white cigarette, lifelessly inserted it into the black lips. Then: a burst of smoke! I could no longer see the figures opposite. I only knew that waves of shameless smoke rings surrounded me, head and face, until, with the shriek of the whistle, I relied on my own strength to struggle out of a small gap and fall out.

Ah! These small figures in the carriage are what I will never forget about the ancient country of the East!

Carrot Top 210

— JULES RENARD, translated by Lin Qu

Carrot Top's Photo Album (Continued)

Twenty-Five

When he was outside, Carrot Top whistled to show that he didn't care about anything. But as soon as he saw the Lepic family following behind him, his whistling stopped abruptly. This made him as sad as breaking a small, worthless whistle in his mouth.

But we must admit that she let him go when he just started to sob.

Twenty-Six

He served as the communication line between his father and mother. Mr. Lepic said to him:

"Carrot Top, this shirt is missing a button."

Carrot Top took the shirt to the Lepic family and said:

"Do I need you to order me around, clown?"

But she took out her sewing basket and sewed on the button.

Twenty-Seven

"If your father wasn't here," the Lepic family shouted, "You would have used a ruthless hand on me a long time ago. You have inserted this knife into my heart and knocked me over on the straw."

Twenty-Eight

"Wipe your nose," the Lepic family often said.

Carrot Top tirelessly wiped it with the edge of his handkerchief. If the handkerchief came apart, he would fold it up again.

Indeed, when he had a cold, the Lepic family put medicine on him, making him so dirty that even his sister Elestine and older brother Felix became jealous. But she specifically added to him:

"This is not so much a fault as it is a benefit. It can make the head clearer."

Twenty-Nine

Because Lepic had been teasing him all morning, Carrot Top couldn't help but say such a terrible thing: "Leave me alone, you stupid thing!"

After saying it, he immediately felt that the surrounding air had frozen, and there were two streams of hot springs in his eyes. He murmured that as long as Lepic made a gesture, he would scamper into the ground.

But Lepic looked at him for a long, long time, but didn't make that gesture.

Thirty

Sister Elestine is getting married soon. The Lepic family allowed him to walk with her fiancé under Carrot Top's supervision.

"Walk in front," she said, "You can jump and play as much as you want!"

Carrot Top walked in front of them, struggling to jump, hesitating. If he forgot to slow down, he could not help but hear some fleeting kisses.

He coughed.

This made him feel stimulated. Suddenly, in front of the village's crucifix, he took off his hat and threw it on the ground, trampled on it with his feet, and shouted:

"Will no one ever love me!"

Immediately, the Lepic family, whose ears were not deaf, stretched out her body from behind the wall, a terrible smile floating on her mouth.

So Carrot Top hurriedly added:

"Except for mom." (End of the manuscript)

According to reports, Tang inspected the provinces and both sides of the Huai River during the two inspections, and Gu inspected central Anhui, southern Anhui, and the areas along the Yangtze River. The detailed situation of the inspection will be released in the inspection report in the future. Now, to put it simply, the secondary education teachers' colleges and middle schools in Anhui are generally well-scaled. The good ones are equal to those in Jiangsu and Zhejiang, while the bad methods are outdated and need to be improved. There are eight vocational schools. The First Vocational School is relatively better, but most of them are not well managed, the equipment is insufficient, and they focus on theory, which is not much different from ordinary middle schools. This is the biggest problem. Compared with central Anhui and southern Anhui, the atmosphere in southern Anhui is better, and the people running schools are very enthusiastic. Hu Ziheng, the principal of the Second Middle School, has been running the school for 20 years. When he was about to hand over, the province still owed 20,000 to 30,000 yuan. He gave the remaining funds from previous years, 70,000 yuan, to the successor. He can manage and build without using special public funds, which is truly commendable. In addition, Hu Jiajian, the principal of the Fourth Middle School in Xuancheng, is also very enthusiastic. The social education in the province is in its infancy, and there are not many mass schools. However, Director Wang of the Second Mass Education Museum in Wuhu can still work hard, and the quality and quantity of social education have been expanded, which has a great impact on the society. As for the local education situation, the local primary schools along the Yangtze River are not only inferior to Jiangsu and Zhejiang, but also to Shandong and Hebei. Compared with the south and north of the Yangtze River, the funding in the north of the Yangtze River is worse, but the education is better than in the south of the Yangtze River. Hong, the Director of Education in Qingyang County along the Yangtze River, is quite capable of rectifying the situation. The schools do not owe salaries, and there are more than 10,000 yuan in savings for expansion expenses. The rest of the counties owe salaries for four or five months at most, and two or three months at least. The local education in each county did not have a fixed budget before. Now, the funds are being tightened and reorganized to clear the arrears. The situation of county education administration is generally better for those with directors, worse for counties with commissioners, and extremely bad in Huizhou. This is because the fourth section of the county has two directors, one in charge of construction and one in charge of education. In addition, there are no supervisors to urge administration, and this commissioner is not a person who has been running schools, so there is no way to improve education. The education funding in the province, the special tobacco tax is collected and managed by the government, and the government allocates 100,000 yuan per month, accounting for two-thirds of the provincial education funding. The funding is relatively stable, but the original temporary fee of 100,000 yuan is withdrawn from the provincial treasury and cancelled invisibly. All schools have regular expenses, but no temporary expenses, which greatly affects equipment construction.

Zhu Sen and Others Talk About the Results of the Investigation

(Telegram from Nanjing, 2nd) The Central Research Institute previously sent Meng Xianmin and others to investigate the geology of the Nanling Mountains. Recently, Zhu Sen and Li Yuyao have returned to Beijing and told reporters that the Tuojiang River in the Nanling Mountains can be used for water conservancy development. The mineral products in the Mengzhu Mountains and Xiaoshui River area, the tin sand in Linwu, and the stone in Qitian, as well as the coal in Qitian Yizhang, have not been mined due to geographical and human relations. A "Nanling Orogeny" was newly discovered in the Nanling Mountains. The orogeny is the orogeny between the Triassic and Jurassic periods. The paleobiological relics of the Nanling Mountains have fossils from the Silurian to the Jurassic periods, and most of them are detached from the parent rock and are extremely precious. Distinguished Sports Book "Middle School Sports Meet Guide" Published 235

Middle school physical education connects the past and the future, serving as the center of school physical education. It occupies the most important position in the overall national physical education. Therefore, in recent times, middle school sports meets have sprung up like mushrooms, becoming more prosperous day by day. However, there is no specialized book on how to organize sports meets. For those in charge of preparations, it takes a lot of thought, and even the results are inevitably not without flaws. Now, the Commercial Sports Meet Guide, newly published by the Diligence Bookstore at 392 Labor Shenfu Road, French Concession, Shanghai, is authored by Wang Fudan, the principal of Jiangnan Sports Teachers College. Mr. Wang based the book on his teaching experience and many years of experience in organizing middle school sports meets. The content is substantial, and the writing is concise. The entire book consists of eleven chapters, each further divided into sections. Chapter 1: The timing of sports meet events; Section 1: Spring sports meet; Section 2: Autumn sports meet; Chapter 2: Sources of funding for sports meets; Chapter 3: Sports meet budget; Chapter 4: Competition methods; Chapter 5: Regulations; Chapter 6: Athlete's guide; Chapter 7: Organizational law of the preparatory committee; Section 1: Duties of the competition division; Section 2: Duties of the venue division; Section 3: Duties of the administrative division; Chapter 8: Middle school joint sports meet; Section 1: Confrontational sports meet; Section 2: Triangular sports meet; Section 3: Joint sports meet; Chapter 9: Equipment; Chapter 10: Group performances; Chapter 11: Forms, and also with many clear illustrations. It is extremely valuable and is the only specialized book for organizing middle school sports meets. All physical education departments and physical education directors of national provincial, municipal, and county middle schools, as well as personnel who organize middle school sports meets, can purchase this book and handle everything with ease and achieve satisfactory results. Wimbledon Sixth Day Men's and Women's Singles Each Eliminate Down to Final Eight 236

Vances Defeats German Polun With Torrential Ball Play 237

(London, 1st, Reuters) The Wimbledon World Tennis Championships continued today in dazzling sunshine. A tide of spectators surged in, and all tickets were sold out five hours after the gates opened. (1) Vances (USA) defeated Polun (Germany), 6-3, 6-2, 6-4.

(3) Austin (England) defeated Spencer (South Africa), 6-2, 6-2, 6-4.

French Davis Cup star Ke Xian defeated American youth Jones three to one, 6-4, 6-8, 8-6, 6-0. Jones is only twenty years old and is the Cambridge University tennis champion in England. Jones' serve is unique at Wimbledon. Several times, his serve was so swift and direct that it surpassed Tilden's cannonball serve in its golden age. After Ke Xian won the first set, Jones fought bravely in the second set for a long time and finally won it back. In the third set, Jones took a 4-1 lead, but Ke Xian was steady and calm, winning 8-6. In the final set, Jones was exhausted and completely defeated.

Austin's Ball Has Rhythm 241

British Davis Cup player Austin defeated South African Spencer in straight sets without much effort. Austin's strokes have rhythm. Although Spencer lost, he still met the challenge unyieldingly. The scores were 6-2, 6-2, 6-4. As for Vances' victory over Polun, it was very easy.

Special Article

Economical Schools and Classes - Hu Jingxi 250

Since the Ministry of Education issued an order that schools should adopt a two-part system and a half-day system, various cities and counties are preparing to try it out in the next semester.

In fact, the two-part system and the half-day system will inevitably slightly discount the progress of children's studies.

I have long had an idea to open up a new path in addition to the two-part system and the half-day system. Now, taking this opportunity, I will first publish the outline of this idea here as a small suggestion.

(1) Mobile Classes in Urban Schools

(1) Use occasions such as large auditoriums, dining halls, sports grounds, campuses, specialized rooms, and empty classrooms when changing classrooms to recruit several classes with mobile teaching locations.

(2) The teachers in mobile classes should follow the principle of two classes and three teachers, taking turns to rest. From the time the children enter school to the time they are dismissed, there is always one person accompanying them in their activities.

(3) The children's activity time and curriculum are the same as those of ordinary classes.

(4) In principle, no office expenses are paid except for teachers' salaries.

(5) Each child should have a hardwood box that can store all used books and objects at ordinary times, and can be used as a short stool when there is no seat.

(2) Mobile Schools in Rural Areas

(1) There is no need for fixed school buildings, and empty houses such as the living rooms in children's homes and ancestral halls in the area are used as temporary teaching places. It is best to have the children's families take turns to provide these, and to implement outdoor teaching more often.

(2) Families who can take turns to provide the space are exempt from their children's tuition fees. (3) The income from tuition fees is used to purchase necessary school equipment. In principle, no office expenses are paid except for teachers' salaries.

(4) There are no fixed holidays. During busy farming seasons, teachers should tour around to guide children and assist their parents in their work.

(5) Because teachers are close to families, they can naturally take on the responsibility of popular education. The most popular books among the Chinese people are almanacs, and guiding adults to read can start from the almanac.

Page 17

Spring and Autumn

Blood and Money 251

— Zui Chi Sheng

Blood is the most precious thing in the human body; without blood, one will wither and die. "Money" is also the most precious thing in life; without money, one will be poor and starve to death. In fact, it can also be said that money is blood, and blood is money. Poor people exchange sweat and blood for money, which is one example. There are also a few terms used by "Bai Xiang" people (Shanghai slang for loafers or gamblers): when there is a lot of money, it is called "blood is strong." Squeezing you for money is called "bleeding." Empty pockets are called "dry blood consumption." This is also clear proof that blood represents money.

Now that science is prosperous, the relationship between "blood and money" has become even closer. If a rich person loses blood and gets sick, they can pay a doctor to transfuse blood. Pumping A's blood into B's blood vessels will restore health. In European and American countries, there are strong poor people who often ask hospitals to sell their blood. In this way, the blood of the poor can be exchanged for the money of the rich. The money of the rich can be exchanged for the blood of the poor. With money, there is no fear of not having blood. A few days ago, the newspaper reported the news that "Duan Zhiquan's blood transfusion was healthy"; the blood he transfused was just the blood of his nephews and nieces. I think this trend is gradually opening up. If ordinary wealthy people are physically weak and suffer from anemia, they can turn danger into safety and prolong their lives. This is really a blessing for the rich.

I also have a plan; in prosperous cities, it is possible to open a real and authentic human blood company, hiring doctors to manage blood testing, blood transfusions, and other procedures. Collect the blood of the poor, preserve it scientifically, and sell it at a marked price so that it can be transfused into the noble bodies of the rich. It doesn't matter if the poor are thin, as long as the rich are fat. It is certain that business will flourish and the door will be like a market. Because the lives of the rich are the most important, with blood, there is no fear of Yama, the king of hell, sending an invitation. Buying and selling human blood, using each other for their own purposes, is a newly invented "way to make money" in the civilized world!

A Brief Discussion on the Various Names for Excrement 252

— Li Pengxiang

Defecation is something that everyone does every day. Although the matter is simple, the names are varied. Each name can represent each class. Now I will briefly discuss what I know, with some textual research in between, but I dare not have the heart of "covering" Mr. Hu Shih's "Lushan Travel Notes" with a lot of textual research.

Wash hands: Among these types of names, this can be considered the most elegant. Foreigners do not say "defecate," but say "wash hands." The English name is Wash Hands. Generally, "higher-class Chinese" use it a lot to show civilization.

Large release: In peacetime, this is not often called, except when Chinese and foreign doctors are treating patients. For example, asking: "Is the large release smooth?" "After eating these pills (or plasters), the large release may be smooth," etc. The sister term of "large release" is "small release." Release means to remove.

Climbing the pit: This name is said to have originated in the north and spread to the Jiangnan area. In the Beiping area, even in homes, they generally do not use what we call "chamber pots" here, because they think it is unhygienic. Everywhere there are rough toilets. This rough toilet, the so-called "pit," cannot be sat on, but can only be "climbed" (or squatted) to "excrete": hence the origin of this name. "Middle-class Chinese" like to call it this.

Going to the restroom: Among the former Qing scholars who generally grew their fingernails long, this "going to the restroom" occupied a large force. However, it is not known whether this "restroom" character is wrong. However, reading Mr. Chen Wangdao's book "An Introduction to Rhetoric," there is an entry on the rhetorical device of "inversion." Its definition is: what the speaker means in their mouth is completely opposite to what they mean in their heart, which is called "inversion." Then this so-called "restroom" is actually the "disrespect" that is in the heart. This can also be said to make sense.

Also, in Mr. Yu Dafu's "Nine Kinds of Diaries," page 4, there is the statement "The weather is very clear and crisp, when going out to the restroom..." After much textual research, I feel that there are generally no errors, so I will record it here for the contemporary sages to judge.

The most undesirable is to come up with the most vulgar and low-class "excrement." Generally, "illiterate" lower-class Chinese like to say "I'm going to excrete." and "Are you going to excrete? Let's go together." etc. nasty words. "Higher-class Chinese" cover their noses and pass by when they hear it. In this area, I am afraid that it will damage "face," so I will not discuss it in detail.

Avoiding Water Ballad 253

— Qing Qu

For days on end, the sky is gloomy and the rain is heavy. The God of Waves is acting evil, the Shang Yang dance. The licentious water seeps and nourishes, the ditches and gullies are full, rushing to protect the embankments, the danger is especially near. Where does the gurgling sound come from? Hearing it, the alarm sounds and people tell each other. The water level of the Great River suddenly overflows. The lower reaches are submerged into courtyards and households. The wind and waves roar without a moment's rest. Avoiding water is like avoiding a tiger. The wall of the east family collapsed again. The western neighbor's mother calls out to her father. This is the year that is suffering from floods. Could it be that the disaster is a catastrophe? The rising tide continues to rise. Dragons and fish swallow each other. Alas, those water people have nowhere to live. It is truly like fish swimming in broken tiles. Moreover, a vast expanse of water. Drifting and moving home without oars. How can such flesh and blood endure the cold? The sight is so terrible that I can't bear to look at it. When you are about to be drowned and buried by fish, who says flood prevention and blocking? Alas, why is the heart not benevolent? Drought and waterlogged, crying and suffering. May I ask why the torrents come. The responsibility lies with the government. How can I get the heavens and Songyue to create a god of water management like Yu?

Envying Those Friends Who Sleep in the Open Air 254

— Rong Yu

A pillow of snores, comfortable and relaxed, this sleep is the most comfortable and enjoyable thing in life; it is also an indispensable page in the history of life.

The old boss in the Western-style house wants to sleep, and the poor devil in the pigeon loft also wants to sleep. When you fall asleep, poverty and wealth are the same, and joys and sorrows are equal. In the rich man's dream, he is kidnapped for ransom, the business he created fails, and the concubine runs away with someone. How can his spirit be at peace? In the poor man's dream, he wins a Champagne ticket: he gets the first prize in an airline ticket, although it is empty joy, he gets temporary joy. So sleeping is the most fair, impartial and unbiased thing. These days, the weather is so hot that there are friends in the pavilion room and the mezzanine floor who have the pain of wanting to sleep but not being able to. The day before yesterday, I went to Shanghai to see a friend. It was night, and I couldn't go back, so he let me stay there. I was used to the countryside, and when I arrived at the narrow and cramped house, it was as hot as a steamer. I couldn't fall asleep in bed, listening to it striking eleven o'clock, twelve o'clock. Later, the lights went out, and it seemed like a speck of dust fell on my face. When I touched it with my hand, it turned into something strangely smelly and soft, followed by my body and feet. I knew that the bedbugs were giving the order for a general attack. I held a non-resistance doctrine, quietly put on my clothes, and circled on the road. It was late at night, but a temporary open-air hotel was opened on the sidewalks on both sides. Some had a rattan chair; some had a wooden plank; some had spread a torn mat on the cement. Everyone was snoring loudly, and their dreams were sweet.

When I saw these people sleeping comfortably, it made me feel the pain of not being able to sleep. They have no bedbug attacks; no hot air steaming. Although it is said that the night is cold and the dew is easy to get sick, damn it, is it more likely to get sick if you are bitten by bedbugs and steamed by hot air? I was happy to get some sleep. My eyes were a little unsustainable: my feet were a little sore. Go back to sleep! How can I endure those bedbugs and hot air? I wish I could discuss it with the friends who sleep in the open air: "Hey! Friends, move aside a little and let me lie down!" But how can I do it in reality!

The Sounds of a Fragrant Night 255

— Tu Chonglou

Although I live in a concession managed by foreigners, my residence is located in an area where my people gather, so every midnight, various sounds are freely transmitted to my bedroom along the road. "Clang," the iron gate of the X Mansion opened! "Whoosh," the motor of the car started.

"Rickshaw, British note? British note?" The maid of XX No. was calling in Yangzhou Shanghai dialect.

"Damn it, don't get run over by a car!" A rickshaw puller grabbed the business, and the remaining rickshaw pullers cursed loudly like this.

"Sir! Madam! If there is any leftover tea and rice, give the poor a bite and a half bowl..." The sad tune came from the beggar's broken throat.

"The beauties of the Peach Blossom River are many, thousands of peach blossoms, not as many as beauties!..." The radio broadcast was much louder than the phonograph.

"Ahang, come back! Amao,..." This is the cry coming from the nearby alley. It is said that calling like this can call back the soul of a seriously ill child who is about to die?

"Dong dong" The sound of the wooden fish. The old monk in the deep white clouds also came to join in the fun in the prosperous city.

"Peng peng..." One machine bicycle after another drove by. "Woo woo..." One car after another drove by.

These noisy and chaotic sounds play in my ears every day. Although I hate them so much, they always surround me.

All the sounds of midnight! When will I be able to leave my ears forever?

Women's Paradise

The Physical Constitutions of Three Types of Women 257

Recently, various countries have paid close attention to research on women's physical constitutions. Generally, women's physical constitutions can be divided into three types in terms of form: the weak type, the athletic type, and the obese type.

The weak type is what is known as the "willowy waist" constitution. The body is thin and long, the skeleton is weak, the neck and limbs are slender, the chest is flat, the skin appears pale, the muscles are relaxed, there is little subcutaneous fat, the muscles are underdeveloped, the body weight is very light, there is little tension throughout the body, and the person is often hunched over. This posture accounts for about 50 to 60 percent of women. The obese type is exactly the opposite of the previous type. The subcutaneous fat is very developed, the body is fat, and there is often the distress of being trapped in excessive fat, hindering the nutritional needs and supply relationships. The nutrients obtained every day are converted into fat. This type can be further divided into alimentary obesity and constitutional obesity. Alimentary obesity is caused by greedily eating more food than is necessary for nutrition, and doing nothing all day except eating. The nutrients obtained are rarely consumed, thus becoming inactive obesity. In other words, they are like pigs. Generally, women with this constitution have reduced reproductive function. Although they appear healthy on the outside, they are actually more prone to illness than thin and tall people.

The athletic type has well-developed bones and muscles. The muscle fiber tissue throughout the body is very tight, the skin is resilient, the shoulders are broad, and the chest is developed. This can be called a complete and beautiful physique. The above three types are only classified based on general appearance. However, when divided in detail, there are hundreds of different types due to each person's acquired and personal characteristics, family circumstances, and so on.

Bad Breath in Women 258

— Bing Yu

Bad breath is most annoying, especially as a major obstacle to closeness between men and women. Love is often estranged by bad breath, and even a beautiful appearance is diminished by it. It is said that when Emperor Xuanzong of Tang first obtained Yang Guifei, he found her appearance indeed charming, but she had bad breath. Later, a court physician advised Guifei to eat more fresh lychees, and gradually the bad breath disappeared. Nowadays, in social circles, eight or nine out of ten women have bad breath. Most of these people are unaware of their problem. Even if someone points it out, they only use some chewing gum to temporarily mask it, without understanding the fundamental source of the problem. According to medical research, bad breath can be caused by diseases of the stomach, intestines, and respiratory system, which can be understood by breathing through the nose. However, in ordinary people, bad breath is mostly caused by tooth decay. To test for cavities, you can insert a toothpick into the tooth hole. If the toothpick smells bad, it can be determined that there are tooth worms at work in the tooth hole. Other causes include not rinsing the mouth after eating, which leads to food residue getting stuck in the teeth, decaying and fermenting, and a clear juice flowing out of the teeth, causing a foul odor. Or it may be caused by alveolar pyorrhea, where tartar accumulates on the teeth and decays, causing a foul odor. There is also a type of stomatitis that causes particularly bad breath. Therefore, for people with bad breath, the first thing to do is to treat the root of the tooth, the second is to immediately brush the mouth and clean the gaps between the teeth after each meal, and the third is to prepare a deodorant mouthwash, such as a thousand-fold solution of potassium permanganate or a five-fold solution of Oxyfull Person to brush the teeth and rinse the mouth with boric acid water. In that case, bad breath can be eliminated.

A Short Account of Sea Bathing at the Beach 259

— Ms. Xu Zhongyang

Mr. Yang Hongkui of the Gaoqiao Seaside Hotel recently invited Mr. Lun Binqi, a swimming champion, to try out sea bathing at the beach. Those who accompanied him included Mr. Wang Weixin, Ms. Bao Lengxue, and myself, among others. We departed by boat at 10 a.m. and arrived at the Gaoqiao pier around 11 a.m. Then, we took a Liuhe Company rickshaw to the Seaside Hotel. Mr. Yang warmly welcomed us and led us on a tour. The new building had just been completed and was richly constructed. Although the sun was scorching hot, a cool breeze gently blew inside the building, which was refreshing. There were more than twenty rooms of various sizes inside, all equipped with modern amenities. A separate room was set aside for showers, especially for rinsing off after sea bathing. Behind the building were vegetable gardens and chicken coops, with many chickens and ducks. Next to the garden was a small pond filled with fish, and there was also a famous chef to provide travelers with delicious food. After lunch, we changed clothes and went to the beach to try out the sea bathing. The water was very warm, unlike pond water, and the white waves were enough to cleanse the body and mind. I was willing and happy to say: "If I could live in a watery town forever, then my wish would be fulfilled." Suddenly, a small red dot appeared from afar. Upon closer inspection, it was a rescue boat, prepared for tourists in case of unforeseen circumstances. We were very impressed with the facilities of the Meibin Hotel. After swimming for two hours, I began to feel tired, so I changed clothes and rested before returning.

Economic Journal, Issue 29, Published Every Monday

Observing the Decline of the Cotton Industry from Cotton Industry Statistics 260

丨Including the Relationship to Rural Revitalization丨 Jiang Dixuan

Cotton is the agricultural product second only to rice and wheat in our country, and textiles are the largest industry in our country, so their rise and fall are closely related to people's livelihoods. In recent years, due to the insufficient price of cotton production, the textile industry has become increasingly depressed, and the import of cotton and cotton goods has increased accordingly. As a result, it directly and indirectly promotes the decline of rural areas. Please explain this.

Cotton goods are the main clothing raw materials in our country, and in the past, most of them relied on imports. Since the outbreak of the European War, the domestic modern textile industry has flourished, and the number of spindles has increased greatly. The import of cotton goods has not continued to increase, but the value still reaches 200 million taels. In recent years, tariffs have been increased repeatedly, and the textile industry seems to be developing again, but the situation is just the opposite. Since the 20th year of the Republic of China, it has been declining, and it has become even worse in recent years. The yarn factory has recently reduced its work. The reason is that the yarn sales are sluggish, and the flowers Customes domestic cotton exceed

Cheap yarn is very expensive, especially zero. Let's examine the recent market prices of standard yarn flowers. In the 18th year of the Republic of China, the average high and low price for the whole year was 162.70 taels for standard yarn and 32.60 taels for standard cotton. In May of this year, the price of standard yarn was 122.40 taels, and the price of standard cotton was 30.20 taels. (The standard grade of this year has been recalculated to be equal to that of the 18th year of the Republic of China.) Compared with each other, the yarn has fallen by 40 taels this year, and the flowers have fallen by 2 taels and 5 cents. With such a depreciation rate, the business of spinning mills can be known. The reason for the cheap yarn is due to the sale. The reason for the high price of flowers is due to the lack of cotton production. Cotton production in our country cannot meet the demand. It began in the 8th year of the Republic of China. The cotton Customs Chao started in the 8th year of the Republic of China. After that, the number of spindles increased, and cotton sales progressed, but cotton production declined instead. The difference between supply and demand became larger and larger, and more and more foreign cotton was imported. The following table shows the supply and consumption of cotton production in our country in the last ten years: (Unit: Dan)

Customs, the net number of imported cotton in the country, excluding exported cotton; spinning factory consumption is the amount used by yarn factories; in addition, cotton used for clothing filling is not included, that is, the difference between supply and consumption. From the above table, it is clear that the quantity of cotton in our country does not meet the demand, and foreign cotton must be used to expand its shortage. The recent surge in imports of foreign cotton is not only limited to the quantity. With social progress, textiles are becoming more refined, the number of yarns is increasing, and raw materials are changing from coarse fleece to fine fleece. The so-called fine fleece that can be used for spinning higher yarn counts in our country is Yangmian produced domestically. According to the survey, the amount of Yangmian was 2,079,543 dan in the 18th year of the Republic of China, 3,169,889 dan in the 19th year, 2,523,650 dan in the 20th year, and 3,065,995 dan in the 21st year, averaging less than 3 million dan per year. Due to the degradation of quality and the blending of coarse cotton by cotton merchants, less than half of these 3 million dan of Yangmian can actually be used for fine yarn spinning, probably no more than 1.5 million dan. Compared with the current number of fine yarns produced in the country, the difference is very large. The following is the ratio of various cottons sold in domestic spinning mills in the last four years:

Chinese Cotton American Cotton Indian Cotton Egyptian Cotton Other

Year 18 68.25 13.66 17.99 0.04 0.0

Year 19 63.11 13.60 22.76 0.21 0.3

Year 20 49.67 26.43 23.2 0.43 0.18

Year 21 52.13 38.58 8.81 0.45 0.03

American cotton and Egyptian cotton are all fine fleece, some of the Chinese cotton is fine fleece, and Indian cotton and other cotton are coarse fleece. In the last four years, the amount of Chinese cotton has decreased, the amount of American cotton has increased sharply, the amount of Indian cotton has decreased greatly in the 21st year, and the increase rate of Egyptian cotton has also increased greatly. This clearly shows the progress in the sale of fine fleece. The fine fleece produced in China is far from enough to meet the demand. This is a special reason for the sharp increase in imports of American cotton in recent years. In the 20th year, the total value of imported foreign cotton was 179,082,246 taels, which jumped to the first place in the customs value of goods. Chinese people have long heard the saying that the customs leakage is the largest for cotton goods. It was unexpected that the rapid progress of cotton would replace the position of cotton goods. This is a huge loss to the national wealth, and its impact on the cotton industry and the decline of rural areas is profound.

The rural economy depends on the export of products to obtain cash to purchase the materials needed. In addition, rural and urban areas are also flowing with gold. In recent years, the quantity of cotton production has been low and has not increased with the spinning. It accounts for half of the textile raw materials taken from abroad, and the cloth woven from this half of foreign cotton is mostly transported to rural areas in the interior. The loss of cotton is completely borne by the rural areas in China. In the 21st year, the value of imported cotton was 180 million taels, which is tantamount to the rural areas having to pay 180 million yuan to make up for the fact that cotton production cannot meet the demand for cloth. The first step of this 180 million taels is from the spinning mill to the outside of the country. The spinning mill weaves the cloth and then transports it to the rural areas to absorb cash to compensate for it. In the ten years from the 12th year to the 21st year, the value of imported cotton was 930 million taels, which is the loss borne by the farmers in terms of clothing due to the fact that they cannot produce the corresponding textile raw materials. In recent years, the business of cotton has not increased, and the number of foreign cotton imported has increased even more. In addition, the two items of rice and wheat are also like this. How can the rural areas not fall into a state of near collapse? At the same time, the textile industry, on the one hand, had to purchase cotton from foreign countries due to the lack of domestic raw materials. The price of foreign cotton is high, and there are taxes on imports, which is enough to make the industry unfavorable. On the other hand, since the rural areas cannot balance the production and consumption of goods, the gold overflows and the financial resources are depleted, and the purchasing power is naturally weak, resulting in a sharp reduction in the demand for yarn and cloth. The stock of yarn in Shanghai has reached as many as 160,000 packages. Therefore, it is said that the decline of the spinning industry and rural areas is directly and indirectly related to the lack of cotton production.

Cotton is the agricultural product second only to rice and wheat in our country, and textiles are the largest industry in the country. Therefore, to rescue the cotton industry, we should pay attention to cotton production, that is, to revitalize the village. Planting cotton is also a key point. If the 4 million dan of cotton imported is produced domestically, the rural areas will increase their income by 180 million yuan, which will benefit the rural economy. It is not a small amount. At the same time, the purchasing power of farmers will increase spontaneously. The 160,000 packages of yarn in Shanghai will also disappear without wings. It is not only possible but also very easy to increase domestic cotton production by 4 million dan. Jiangsu and Hubei provinces have already been called the most famous cotton-producing areas in our country. However, according to the survey, the amount of wasteland in these two provinces that can be reclaimed to plant cotton is even more than the existing cotton field area. The coastal salt reclamation areas in Jiangsu can all plant cotton, and its area is half of the existing cotton field area in the country. The area of Henan and Shaanxi in the northwest is even more countless. My friend Li Guozhen is in charge of planting cotton in Shaanxi and wrote to me that the completion of the Jinghui Canal can increase the cotton area by 3 million mu. However, the domestic cotton production hovers around 8 million dan every year. It is a pity that it is not even close to this. It is not necessary to talk about easy quality and change. There are certainly many reasons for this. Let's divide it into direct and indirect aspects and talk about the most obvious ones.

In the direct aspect, of course, it is the failure to devote efforts to improving cotton planting. The government has no initiative to do it, and the people may have an initiative to do it, but there are various obstacles, so improving cotton planting is just empty talk on paper, and there is very little practical work. The reason why American cotton has today is due to the hard work of the US Department of Agriculture. Looking back at our country, what about it? India has been reduced to a British colony, and there is still a central cotton planting committee. Looking back at our country, what about it? If we can devote a little effort to improving cotton, the benefits are where the people are going. If we guide the situation, the results will be like holding a left coupon. Zhejiang used to produce the roughest and shortest cotton, and only 10 yarns were spun. Now it can also produce cotton that can spin 32 yarns. Hunan used to not produce cotton, but now it produces more than 200,000 dan of cotton, and the quality is also tending to Hubei. Other provinces such as Shandong and Shaanxi have all achieved considerable results, which is also the result of the authorities' slight efforts. Jiangsu has always been the number one cotton-producing area in China, but recently the output and quality have declined. It is not that Jiangsu is suddenly not suitable for planting cotton. It is also because the authorities have ignored it. Now, comparing Jiangsu and Hunan, one advances and the other retreats, what is the relationship between the rural areas and the spinning industry? Therefore, we people can just not raise our voices and sing loudly to rescue the rural areas, so that we can pay a little attention to the rural areas in peacetime, and we will certainly not collapse like this. As for the technical issues of improving cotton planting, there are many reasons. Now I will not discuss them in detail.

Speaking of indirect relations, our country not only fails to devote efforts to improving cotton planting, but there are many things that hinder the development of cotton planting. Let's take the most obvious ones. 1. Cotton areas are mostly in the interior, while spinning mills for selling cotton are in the ports. When cotton is transported from the producing area to the spinning mill, taxes are levied repeatedly, once and again. When cotton is transported from Shaanxi and Henan to the east, the names of the taxes are too numerous to mention. Recently, the business tax has been implemented, and cotton is taxed once every time it changes hands. The burden is almost the same as that of imported foreign cotton. 2. Inconvenient transportation and high freight rates are also reasons that affect the development of cotton production. In a certain year, cotton in Shaanxi was hoarded for three years and could not be transported to the east, and the price was also extremely low. The southeast was in a cotton famine. This situation happens from time to time. Shaanxi is the most suitable for the growth of long-staple cotton, and the domestic demand for long-staple cotton is increasing day by day. Its cotton planting should be developed, but the fact is very different. It is given by many obstacles to transportation. It goes without saying that the freight rate is heavier. From the northwest to Shanghai, the cost is no less than that of American cotton to our country, and there is no guarantee that the route will be blocked. 3. Cotton merchants mix and blend moisture, and the government has issued three orders and five declarations, but has not taken practical measures to ban it. The cotton in Shaanxi and Henan often has lengths of nearly one and a half inches, but it is mixed with cotton that is less than eight points, so that the long fleece also loses its value. Farmers plant long fleece but cannot get the price that long fleece cotton should get, and they cannot put it into practical use, which hinders the improvement of cotton production. Nothing is better than this. There are now inspection bureaus for moisture blending, but manufacturers buy cotton. Penalties are imposed for evil but not rewards for good. For example, if the moisture content of cotton is above 12 catties, the price will be deducted, and if it is below 12 catties, the price will not be increased, so the effect is shallower. For all these reasons, factory owners lament that it is better to use foreign cotton than to use Chinese cotton. The authorities are aiming at tax revenue and freight. I wonder if rural areas will decline and agricultural production will not increase. Taxes and freight will also be reduced to nothing. This policy of draining the pond to catch fish has been in place for a long time, and it is reasonable to create today's situation. Therefore, we must establish a circle and do not have to revitalize and rescue it. We can reasonably and legally rectify the causes of the disease that hinder its progress in the possible scope. The rural areas and the cotton industry will be revived spontaneously.

Special Issue on Cooperative Movement 丨Continued from this Journal on July 1丨

Cooperative Movement and the Transformation of Joint-Stock Companies Wang Zongpei 261

Cooperation is a new economic organization that has emerged in the world in the last 100 years, and it has achieved considerable results in various countries. It has also been officially introduced to China for more than ten years. In the past ten years, scholars have advocated it first, and then the government has promoted it. The cooperative movement has also progressed from the period of publicity and advocacy to the period of practice and organization. The organization and establishment of cooperative societies in various provinces and regions have also shown unprecedented progress. According to the statistics of the 21st year of the Republic of China, there were 2,673 cooperative societies in the country, with a total of 987,788 members. This number seems to be very large, but compared with the national population of 480 million, it only accounts for 2/10,000, which is still a very small number. It is even more impossible to compare it with advanced European countries.

The reason why the cooperative movement cannot be universally developed and receive practical benefits cannot be blamed on the comrades who advocate it. I blame the majority of the people for being A Dou, who is an illiterate. They have never heard of or seen this kind of business since they were born, and there is not a shadow of it in their heads. Therefore, no matter how hard the advocates shout, they are still confused. This kind of work that plays the lute to a cow is of course futile. A part of the advocates had no choice but to adopt a strategy of tempting them with profits, telling them that if they organized a cooperative society, the government could lend them money as capital. These sweets have certainly had considerable effect. Many farmers, with 12 points of hope, established cooperative societies, but unfortunately, the sweets are just a kind of verbal benefit, and many cooperative societies have become statistical records because they cannot borrow money.

Failure is the mother of success. The mistakes of the past have given us many lessons. We know that there is also a kind of cooperative organization among the Jewish people, called Axtia (Axia). This kind of Axia spread from Eastern Europe to Western Europe, and then to Asia and North America. In the second half of the 19th century, the cooperative movement in Europe rose, and followed the trend of the times, Axia was also baptized. Now, many of the Axtias in the United States have gone through registration procedures and become legal organizations, protected by the Credit Union Act. The credit cooperation of Axtia is really a point worth studying in the cooperative movement. The current cooperative system has been introduced to our country for more than ten years. The injected publicity in the past few years has still had very little effect. I remember that Mr. Hu Hanmin once said in "How to Promote Cooperative Undertakings": "Cooperation is a very good term, but we must not be shocked by the good term of cooperation and ignore the inherent cooperative undertakings in our country. The inherent cooperative undertakings in our country, although they do not have the name of cooperation, have the reality of cooperation." Mr. Hu said that "the inherent cooperative undertakings in our country that have the reality of cooperation but not the name of cooperation" is the joint-stock system. He believes that if he can earnestly improve him according to the principles of cooperation and make him truly adapt to the requirements of the people, he will definitely become a good organization for the people to regulate finance.

The joint-stock company is an inherent cooperative system in our country, also known as "gathering", commonly known as "Pan Tao", and some people also use the three words "human character head" as a pronoun. These are all names in the Taihu Lake basin of Jiangnan. In the Huaiyang area of Jiangbei, it is called "inviting meetings"; in the provinces of Anhui, Jiangxi, Hubei, and Hunan, it is called "playing meetings"; in the Jinquyan prefectures of eastern Zhejiang, it is called "gathering meetings", and in the Ningshao area, it is called "jiao meetings". The name in the two Guang provinces is "doing meetings", but Yunnan Province is called "Shehui". Although the words are different, the meaning is the same, and the methods are largely the same. The difference is that the joint-stock companies in various places have some local colors. The size of the joint-stock, the length of the meeting period, the number of members, and the level of interest are somewhat different.

Although the joint-stock company is said to have different methods in different places, the meaning and spirit are consistent. We should also give this praiseworthy inherent cooperative system a cooperative baptism, just like the Axtia, so that he can establish a rising special force for the history of East Asian cooperation. If the cooperative movement can use this kind of folk cooperative foundation, it is tantamount to getting a shortcut to the people, and it will definitely have a great impact on the progress of cooperation.

Speaking of using some joint-stock companies, we must first talk about the current difficulties of cooperative societies. Now the organization of most cooperative societies is nothing more than wanting to borrow some money, so when organizing, they only seek to establish it quickly. The members are naturally randomly gathered, and the society fees are also collected to the minimum extent. Moreover, most of the cooperative societies are of unlimited liability nature due to the amount of money borrowed. After the formalities for establishment and registration are completed, whether they have borrowed money or not, they will probably not plan the progress of the society affairs any more. Therefore, the society shares of cooperative societies that have been established for one or two years are still the previous numbers, and there are no records of savings. What is the use of this kind of cooperative society that only knows how to rely on others and does not seek independence?

To establish a solid foundation for cooperative undertakings, we must first correct the mistakes of the past. If cooperative societies want to break a path of survival from the current gloom, they must vigorously implement the savings policy of members, and the application of the joint-stock system is also a method of promoting savings for members. In this way, not only can savings be realized, but also the relationship between members can be strengthened.

If a cooperative society wants to use the joint-stock system to develop its savings business, it cannot swallow the whole thing. It must transform the joint-stock system in moderation so as not to violate the principles of cooperation. Assuming that we take the bidding meeting as the object of transformation, my personal opinion is as follows:

1. Organizational issues. The head meeting organized by the cooperative society is the cooperative society. It is divided into several groups, and the members of each group are limited to members of the cooperative society, from 15 to 20 people. The first phase is collected by the cooperative society as a fund, without interest, and the head of the bidding can also be sent in the future.

2. Meeting funds. The meeting funds of the bidding meeting depend on the economic strength of the members (i.e., the members), at least two yuan and at most ten yuan. A member must recognize at least half a meeting and at most two or three meetings.

3. Meeting period. The meeting period also depends on local habits, at most once a month, or once every two or three months.

4. Bidding head issues. The interest rate of the bidding meeting is stipulated by the cooperative society with very high and very low restrictions, and the maximum and minimum number of bidding heads in each period is calculated according to compound interest. Make sure that you do not suffer losses when you receive first and then receive later. Members cannot exceed the highest limit when bidding. If two or more people bid the highest price, then the recipient of the meeting will be replaced by the second highest bidder. The head of the bidding in each period is kept by the cooperative society and distributed when the meeting is full.

5. Distribution of meeting funds. When a member wins the meeting funds, he must submit 2/10 of the meeting funds, 1/10 to purchase shares of the cooperative society, and another 1/10 as savings deposits. And you must submit a guarantee of considerable value, and a credit guarantee is also possible, before you can receive the money.

This is a rough design, and I hope that the cooperative society will try it out and the experts will give guidance.

Recent European Cooperative Movement (Continued) Peng Shiqin 262

The existing wholesale cooperatives are actively striving to expand wholesale organizations, select central hubs for commerce and transportation, build cooperative sites, construct warehouses, establish factories, and various production organizations. They are also working to unite cooperatives of different types to consolidate the power of the national cooperative movement. The Dutch wholesale cooperative has been established for a long time. Last year, they built a grand wholesale cooperative in Rotterdam. Cooperatives across the country are members of the association. Future development is immeasurable. A country's cooperation can only establish trademarks for goods and proceed to self-production after it has a complete wholesale cooperative. Otherwise, even with sufficient capital, it will be difficult to sustain due to a lack of sales channels. So-called merchant cooperatives are organizations where retail merchants organize and use wholesale methods for joint purchasing. Therefore, the current cooperative movements in various countries, which are dealing with retail merchants, must put all their efforts into promoting wholesale cooperation to make it a complete and sound organization. Thus, this effort by cooperatives is to meet two important internal and external demands.

(4) Implementation of Branch System: The cooperative movement is a product of capitalism, and all measures are changing with each passing day following capitalist enterprise methods. Before the branch system became popular in commerce, cooperatives already had similar organizations. Recently, due to the very developed branch method in commerce, especially in the food sector, cooperatives have paid special attention to the responsible branch system. Large capitalist stores often set up branches in every district of the city and even in various towns across the country from the beginning of their opening. Their goods are either produced by themselves or purchased in bulk. Combined with rationalization in management and transportation, the cost is naturally lower. Moreover, customers can buy what they need anywhere. There is no need to go to places far from home to buy things. After the Swiss consumer cooperative succeeded in the two steps of unification and consolidation, the area where its members are distributed is very wide. If there were no branches, there would be many difficulties. Therefore, this movement has developed rapidly in recent years. When we walked around in Baar, Switzerland, we saw neat and beautiful small shops with red facades everywhere. These are branches of the upper and lower Baar consumer cooperatives. Moreover, there are three or four such branches in one area, separately selling various groceries and other items that can be handled independently. We paid special attention to this trend when investigating the European cooperative movement this time.

(5) Universality of Neutral Tendencies: Cooperation is a free organization that does not ask about political and religious beliefs. Since the Nimes school established the principle of neutrality with consumers as the center, it has been adhered to by cooperatives in various countries. Even cooperatives that are essentially run or controlled by a political party or a religious faction still use neutrality as a slogan on the surface, both to unite internally and to appeal to society. The Belgian cooperative movement is rooted in the Belgian Socialist Party and trade unions. To this day, it still cooperates with political parties and trade unions, which can be said to be a trinity. The Belgian Cooperative Bureau, the central organization of Belgian cooperation, had its leaders tell us last winter about the relationship between political parties and cooperatives, and there were talks about making the two independent. Because past facts tell us that the development of cooperation is often affected by political parties. This influence is only economic. As for the past in Italy, it was simply fundamentally destroyed by politics. This time, when Hitler came to power, although there has been no news about cooperatives, judging from what we heard in Germany, we deeply know that the cooperatives under the Hamburg Consumer Cooperative Union will also share the same fate as the cooperatives in Italy at that time. In short, this principle of neutrality has not seen significant application in practice, but cooperators in various countries are proclaiming it there every day.

This brief introduction cannot be said to have clarified the trends of the European cooperative movement. Readers who are particularly interested in this are hoped to read our "Investigation Report on the European Cooperative Movement," which we are currently drafting, in the future.

Corrigendum: In the Shanghai Cooperative's article, "company asset" should be corrected to "member"

Financial Week Encountered Customs Closure, Financial Market Particularly Quiet 264

Yesterday, the silver market was even quieter because it was Sunday and the third day of customs closure. Banks were completely closed, and there were no transactions to record. The silver market was also very flat. Both the morning and afternoon markets were priced at 400%, with few transactions. The volume of note exchange transactions was far less than in previous days. Morning market transfers were over 4.9 million, new transactions were 700,000 to 800,000. Afternoon market transactions were over 400,000. Small guild transactions were over 600,000. The exchange of silver receipts at money shops was over 2.9 million, also less than the previous day. According to industry insiders, the new currency was originally scheduled to be issued in the market the day before yesterday, but it has now been changed to the 4th due to the bank closure. Jiangnan small silver was priced at 845 yuan in both the morning and afternoon markets, down 2 yuan from the previous day. Morning market transactions were 6,000 角. A Picture of Life: The Small Vegetable Market 268

-- Yao

I have had the determination to visit the small vegetable market for a long time; there is no gathering place for selling vegetables, fish, and meat in the townships, so it is no wonder that people in the countryside are curious about the small vegetable market in big cities. Finally, on a Sunday morning, I stepped into the small vegetable market!

There are various stalls here, some selling fresh fish, some selling fresh meat, fresh shrimp, etc. There are various different loads, some with beans, some with vegetables, some with melons. Judging from the facial expressions of the various vendors, I know that they are all expecting to have more customers than usual today -- just like farmers expect a bountiful autumn harvest. Some are shouting with all their might how cheap and how good their goods are to attract customers. Some are sprinkling water on their goods, and some are putting ice on them, in order to sell well -- or because of a difference of one or two copper coins, the transaction cannot be completed. Conflicts over prices lead to quarrels and even turn into a full-scale brawl. On the buying side, there are merchants' wives who can barely make a living, haggling over prices and weighing goods everywhere, trying to get some cheap goods. There are cooks and maids from mansions, discussing with them what to buy today to please their masters and get some kickbacks for themselves. Each one is holding on to their money tightly, unwilling to easily complete a transaction. There are also a few young mistresses and wives who, because they played mahjong for a few rounds the night before, still have their eyelids tightly closed, barely able to bear their fatigue. If you can see how many goods are in her basket when she leaves, you can determine whether her mahjong game last night was a victory or a defeat. There are laborers who have scraped together the number of copper coins they brought to exchange for the leftovers that others have chosen. There are small vendors from Jiangbei, looking like refugees,争奪 (contending) for the yellow leaves peeled off by others and the fresh goods that are rotten and unbearable.

Here, you can clearly see:

The people in the city are also struggling for life in the same way.

The people in the city are also stingy with money in the same way!

Puppets Can Also Start Talking 269

-- Xueying

Puppets, also known as wooden figures, were not originally all made of wood. They could be made of thin leather or hard paper, cut into shapes, etc., placed on top of circles with axle holes left in the center, like wheels. A candle was lit in the middle, and a higher circle coated with white paper was placed on top. Manpower was used to push it, causing it to move forward in a circle, called a leather puppet or a running horse lantern. Although not very common, at least a considerable number of people have seen them.

Another more popular type is the puppet show that people from Jiangbei perform in Shanghai. They do have wood components, and because they are more popular, I won't describe their construction in detail. In the past, you could sometimes see them in the City God Temple or empty wastelands. Now, I'm afraid there are even more! After the January 28th Incident in Zhabei, there were more empty wastelands, so the opportunities to see them are even greater. This also deserves a word of praise for the cleverness of the people of Jiangbei! Inside a roughly five-foot square stage, they hide musical instruments such as gongs and drums. The person controlling the puppet behind it has to make the puppet move, speak, and the gongs and drums sound. This is all supported by just one person, so he can be considered clever. However, the words below, the audience may find even rarer! Because the puppet itself can tell lies.

Before talking about the construction of the puppet that can speak, I have to introduce it again, because its construction is not at all like the two types mentioned above. Although the faces are different, they are like our Southern products, which can be said to be a rare thing. No, people who don't grow up in the South may not have seen it! But now, if you need to see it, there are also places to see it. That is, in the lace shops around the 大白渡桥 (Great White Bridge), they call it Mandarin-doll. I heard that foreigners are now buying them to put at home as Joss to worship, learning our noble Chinese customs. But they only use fresh flowers, 清香 (incense), and 白臘 (white wax). Now I have to add that those sold are only the embryos used for puppet shows in the South. They have not yet been fitted with the handle that controls their movements. There are a total of three handles for controlling the movements, made of iron or bamboo. One is installed on the back of the body to support her so that she can stand freely. The other two are installed on her left and right hands respectively. These are a bit more troublesome than the Jiangbei people's, because each person can only operate one. Speaking, of course, also has to be done by someone else. It's simply all controlled by the person behind, a bit like the double act in the 大世界 (Great World), but the puppet show is very small.

Recent puppet shows are becoming more and more advanced. Those old-fashioned ones are probably not as good! They are indeed much more advanced. Now, the three handles behind the puppet are also trained to speak. There is no need for the person behind to control them, and they can also propose and preside. However, in this modern age of 科舉 (imperial examination) prosperity, this is not a strange thing. What we should be surprised at is that the puppet itself speaks and argues with the handles about who is right and wrong. The audience must want to hear what she said, right? Let me write it below: "You are doing things that will drive us to extinction, calling me to take the blame. What's the point of this? Be more content and leave some room for your descendants... You are relying on the Guandong Army to be in charge. Why are you looking for me? I quit." See the 北平 (Beiping) correspondence in the Shen Bao of the 27th (赵欣伯 (Zhao Xinbo), 熙洽 (Xi Qia), and 郑孝胥 (Zheng Xiaoxu) are investigating and sealing up the properties of former dignitaries in the three northeastern provinces in the puppet state of Manchukuo, and encouraging the heads of the Guandong Army to handle everything...). The fact is so strange. Although modern science is prosperous and puppets have been invented to be like living people, if the three handles do not cooperate with the puppet, they will probably still become waste. You who control it from behind, although you can make good use of waste, you are still not clever enough, unlike our Jiangbei people!

Correspondence from Shop Assistants

Youth Morality and Vigilante Corps 270

Editor Sir:

We see that the current social environment is changing day by day, constantly turning towards that dark and lightless road; it has led to the people of today also following its transformation. People's hearts are getting worse day by day; especially our young men and women, their moral character has also deteriorated. Tempted by the social trends, it has led many promising young people to turn into base people; alas! Society has reached such a state, it is really terrible! Because of this, I want to organize a "Youth Moral Vigilante Corps" to warn these young people to go towards the bright road. Do you think this organization is good? Does it have any relationship with the law? Please teach me well! With sincere wishes for a pleasant summer. Respectfully, Tian Yuqing.

Editor's reply: The fact that the morals of young people are deteriorating day by day is indeed a great danger to the future of the nation. I admire Tian Jun's vision in wanting to find a way to correct this. However, the method proposed by Tian Jun is really not permitted by law. The improper behavior of young people in general now has not yet reached the point of violating the law, or even if they have violated the law, what they have committed is a private accusation crime. Unless they are directly harmed, other people have no right to consult. Therefore, it is illegal for you to organize a vigilante corps to interfere with them. If you don't do it well, you will be violating regulations such as "infringement of freedom" and "infringement of privacy." We believe that since the purpose of this society is legitimate, it can be slightly changed so that it will not be prohibited by law. First, the name of this corps should be changed to something like Youth Encouragement Corps. Second, the scope of vigilance should be limited to members who have filled out a volunteer form. Third, if you think that its effectiveness is too small in this way, then you can use the method of propaganda to expand the number of members.
